id='poem_sentence_6_1208401_comment'></div>恭惟陛下久处潜藩，充养圣德，亦如高宗旧劳于外；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208401_comment'></div>春秋鼎盛，历数在躬，亦如三君自外而入；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208401_comment'></div>置《无逸》于座右，采唐、汉之所长，则文、宣、太宗之事，盖有灿然可观者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208401_comment'></div>神考所谓「吾无间然」者，臣愚愿有稽焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1208401_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208409' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208409' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208409?labeling=true' target='_blank'>言蔡京劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208409")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208409_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208409'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208409'>臣闻事有大小，言有先后，事之大者，言之所当先也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208409_comment'></div>臣伏见翰林学士承旨蔡京久在朝廷，为害甚大，今所当言，无先于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208409_comment'></div>绍圣之初，常安民为御史，京为安民所击，得罪赎铜，因与安民有隙，离间谮诉，无所不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208409_comment'></div>自逐去安民，而朝廷耳目于是蔽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208409_comment'></div>去年邹浩之狱，天下震骇，人皆归罪于两惇，孰知其事始于京之去安民也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208409_comment'></div>今朝廷大政又皆委曲迁就，而为一京之地，公议詾詾，人不敢言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208409_comment'></div>臣若畏祸缄默，恐负陛下，今所当言，其有先于此乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208409_comment'></div>夫国之大事，无过宗庙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208409_comment'></div>可传万世，无过信史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208409_comment'></div>今京以矫诬之言，唱西宫之事，妄托先训，以胁上下，自改《裕录》，以实其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208409_comment'></div>朝廷遂信其说，欲迁神考于西宫，岂非以朝廷大政委曲迁就而为一京之地乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208409_comment'></div>京在绍圣中，亲入文字，请灭刘挚等家族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208409_comment'></div>其言所以不行者，哲宗之大惠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208409_comment'></div>今哲宗之大惠不闻于天下，而京复自谓有究治平反之力，欲使天下皆谓哲宗有滥诛之意，而京有及物之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208409_comment'></div>始则为国生事，以复私雠，今则归过先朝，自图身利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208409_comment'></div>前言既效，今计亦行，岂非以朝廷大政委曲迁就而为一京之地乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208409_comment'></div>陛下善述神考，钦承哲宗，至德美意达于天下，而京乃矫诬两朝，上累圣政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208409_comment'></div>如此二事，未免委曲迁就以为京地，况其它乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208409_comment'></div>前日缄口之人，今欲有言于陛下，京在朝廷，则莫不以言为戒矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208409_comment'></div>前日沮隔之士，今欲有望于陛下，京在朝廷，则莫不以进为惧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208409_comment'></div>以言为戒，则依旧钳默；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208409_comment'></div>以进为惧，则甘于沉废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208409_comment'></div>天下公议与陛下即政之初，渐不侔矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208409_comment'></div>京之计策渐行，人情之向背渐一，为京之羽翼者渐张，为陛下之耳目者渐沮，朝廷之威自此而渐弱，蒙蔽之患自此而渐成，安危治乱，渐可卜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208409_comment'></div>臣谓方令之患，无大于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208409_comment'></div>臣虽不肖，而所言皆得于公议，陛下黜臣不肖之身可也，因废臣言，则为不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208409_comment'></div>臣愿陛下俯察刍荛之忠，速去腹心之患，独出睿断，正京罪恶，以警天下。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1208409_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208400' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208400' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208400?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谏幸龙德宫观芝草奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208400")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208400_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208400'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208400'>伏闻车驾将幸蔡王外第，都下之人老幼相传，欢呼鼓舞，愿瞻天表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208400_comment'></div>人心所归，于此可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208400_comment'></div>然闻欲因幸龙德宫，而传者以为欲观芝草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208400_comment'></div>窃惟陛下即位以来，天下丰稔，庆瑞已多，芝草虽异，臣知不足以动圣意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208400_comment'></div>况自祖宗以来，乘舆初出，必正其名，若非为民祈祷，即因谒见宗庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208400_comment'></div>今乘舆之出固有名矣，因幸潜宫，何为不可，然而观芝草之嫌，亦不可不恤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208400_comment'></div>此而不恤，流传寖广，天下之人将有不远万里而献芝者矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1208400_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208410' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208410' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208410?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再论蔡京之罪并辞免知无为军奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208410")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208410_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208410'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208410'>臣孤远不肖，误蒙拔擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208410_comment'></div>窃谓陛下既开言路，以防壅蔽，臣职在献替，义当如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208410_comment'></div>乃不能慎默，辄贡不根之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208410_comment'></div>陛下原其用心止为忧国，虽行贬黜，寻复改命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208410_comment'></div>臣蝼蚁之身，将何以上报圣主涵容之私乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208410_comment'></div>臣昨者自闻隔对已后，曾将上殿劄子具状缴进，为言京在绍圣中亲写奏劄，乞诛灭刘挚等家族，赖哲宗仁圣，不行其请；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208410_comment'></div>今京自谓有究治平反之功，欲归过于哲宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208410_comment'></div>又言，京自谓当元丰末命，带开封府刽子携剑入内，欲斩王圭，以沮宣仁怀异之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208410_comment'></div>京自言己有社稷之功，而使宣仁大谤终未辨明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208410_comment'></div>又言，京因不得为执政，与章惇睽绝，今乃欺陛下与惇睽绝者为国事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208410_comment'></div>又言，京为弟卞执政无状，自来不相往来，以欺陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208410_comment'></div>又言，京欲独擅史局，妄有奏请，以致《哲宗实录》不差正官修撰，轻一朝大典，违祖宗故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208410_comment'></div>又言，京所荐引，得美官、在要路者不下数百千人，其间多有才智艺能之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208410_comment'></div>若京在朝廷，则此数百千人者皆指为蔡氏之党；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208410_comment'></div>京去朝廷，则此数百千人者皆为朝廷之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208410_comment'></div>然则广收人才，消合朋党，唯在去京而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208410_comment'></div>又言，京关通交结，其势益牢，广布腹心，羽翼成就，愚弄朝廷，有同儿戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208410_comment'></div>陛下若不早悟，渐成孤立，后虽悔之，亦无及矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208410_comment'></div>臣上件劄子所言，在既责扬州粮料院以前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208410_comment'></div>陛下若以臣言为是，则当如臣所请，按京之罪，明正典刑，然后改差遣以示听纳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208410_comment'></div>若以臣言为非，同是臣事发更为，其罪益大，重加贬窜，乃得允当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208410_comment'></div>今京桀骜自肆，无所畏惮，而臣章屡上，未蒙降出，则是陛下不以臣言为信矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208410_comment'></div>不信其言而轻于改命，传之天下，人必骇惑，其为初政之累，莫大于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208410_comment'></div>且京久在朝廷，专以轻君罔上为能，以植党任奸为术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208410_comment'></div>挟继述之说，为自便之计，稍违其意，则以不孝不忠之名胁持上下，决欲取胜而后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208410_comment'></div>主威不行，士论忧恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208410_comment'></div>今京不出，必为心腹之患，宗社安危，未可知也，臣一身迁贬危辱，何足道哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1208410_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1208410'><span class='label'>按：</span>此奏《历代名臣奏议》亦误作任伯雨上。按《通鉴长编纪事本末》一二九：元符三年九月「丁亥，诏新添差监扬州粮料院陈瓘知无为军。时瓘已出国门，即于门外露章辞免」，以下即引此奏。可知为陈瓘之露章奏。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1208410_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1208411' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208411' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208411?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论蔡京交结外戚奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208411")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208411_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208411'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208411'>臣近为言事不根，谪授监扬州粮料院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208411_comment'></div>受告方得数日，便蒙改差知无为军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208411_comment'></div>闻命皇惑，唯知感涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208411_comment'></div>臣闻圣人之过也，如日月之食焉，人皆见之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208411_comment'></div>及其更也，人皆仰之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208411_comment'></div>朝廷以一时之怒，黜忠谏之臣，此如日月之食也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208411_comment'></div>今兹改命，可见圣人之心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208411_comment'></div>天下有识之人，谁不叹仰！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208411_comment'></div>岂独贱臣一身之私幸乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208411_comment'></div>臣虽上感圣恩，而未敢便受新命者，诚有说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208411_comment'></div>明道中，仁祖欲率群臣为皇太后上寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208411_comment'></div>范仲淹谏曰：「人主无北面之礼」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208411_comment'></div>明肃大怒，而仲淹得罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208411_comment'></div>元祐中，蔡确之贬，范纯仁以为不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208411_comment'></div>宣仁大怒，而纯仁得罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208411_comment'></div>此二臣者，可黜可逐，而尊主不贰之心，不可以威势夺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208411_comment'></div>方刘氏甚危之日，极力救护，却是仲淹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208411_comment'></div>以宣仁晚年，翻然远虑，复思纯仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208411_comment'></div>知忠言之有益于国家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208411_comment'></div>大抵忠臣之心，唯欲保全国体，为千万年久长之虑，岂忍使天下议论及于慈闱！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208411_comment'></div>今宗良等内外交通，迹状甚明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208411_comment'></div>蔡京交结之迹，天下所共知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208411_comment'></div>京作《向縡墓志》曰：「吾平生与士大夫游，无如承旨蔡公与我厚者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208411_comment'></div>京为从官，而与外戚相厚，书于碑刻，以自矜夸，如此之类，非止一事而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208411_comment'></div>又京与弟卞久在朝廷，同恶相济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208411_comment'></div>卞则出矣，京则牢不可拔，自谓执政可以决取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208411_comment'></div>人皆谓京因慈云寺得裴彦臣交结之助，外议讻讻，众所知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208411_comment'></div>京作《向宗良麻词》云：「元丰末命，尝有嘉言」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208411_comment'></div>嘉言若出于宗良，则大谤必归于宣仁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208411_comment'></div>京亦自谓，曾带开封府刽子，携剑入内，欲斩王圭，以沮宣仁怀异之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208411_comment'></div>京以禁中疑似之传，书于制命，扬于天庭，自谓与宗良皆社稷之功，而使宣仁负无穷之谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1208411_comment'></div>京之谄事外戚，不畏上天，一至如此，岂惟有害于朝廷，实亦无益于外家！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1208411_comment'></div>臣尽忠于陛下，尽忠于皇太后，所以言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1208411_comment'></div>皇太后圣德大功，冠绝今古，陛下承颜养志，方以大舜、武王为法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1208411_comment'></div>入修家人之礼，则恭顺无阙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1208411_comment'></div>出治朝廷之事，则威柄不分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1208411_comment'></div>大舜、武王之孝，何以加于此乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1208411_comment'></div>京所谓孝则不然，但欲陛下授柄于外家而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1208411_comment'></div>此蔡氏之利，非宗社之福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1208411_comment'></div>陛下以圣德嗣位，春秋方富，如汉文帝、宣帝即位之年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1208411_comment'></div>尽孝于东朝，励精于政事，独操大柄，足以有为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1208411_comment'></div>而京之所以胁持陛下者，原其用意，谓陛下未可以独为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1208411_comment'></div>哲宗躬揽之初，圣意本无适莫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1208411_comment'></div>章子厚虽挟功自恣，然其初犹有兼取元祐之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1208411_comment'></div>自京、卞首发邪论，盗攘国柄，凡有所请，必以继述为说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1208411_comment'></div>稍违其意，则欲以不忠之名加于上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1208411_comment'></div>假朝廷之诛赏，示私门之好恶，轻君误国，首尾八年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1208411_comment'></div>至于今日，狃于故态，又以此意胁持陛下，傅会继述之论，假托报功之说，密持离间之谋，伺察陛下，包藏祸心，若有所待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1208411_comment'></div>京之出言用意，谅无逃陛下之圣察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1208411_comment'></div>且陛下述神考之圣德，报太母之大功，岂独陛下之私心，是亦臣子之所愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1208411_comment'></div>合臣子之所愿，尽四海之欢心，然后陛下有庆，兆民赖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1208411_comment'></div>天子之孝，孰大于此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1208411_comment'></div>今京所赖，非兆民之所同赖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1208411_comment'></div>陛下一违京意，则京必以不孝之名责陛下矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1208411_comment'></div>陛下徇一京胁持之私名，而不畏天下至公之大义乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1208411_comment'></div>畏天下至公之大义，当流窜蔡京，以安国家而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1208411_comment'></div>臣前日之言不负天，不负陛下，不负皇太后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1208411_comment'></div>果蒙陛下移臣差遣，若非皇太后察臣之忠，陛下必不欲如此旨挥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1208411_comment'></div>然而京在朝廷，则家国未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1208411_comment'></div>臣虽移得差遣，有何安乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1208411_comment'></div>臣之不敢受命者，其说如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1208411_comment'></div>臣露章所言，未甚子细；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1208411_comment'></div>复以此章干渎圣听，所以尽惓惓之诚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1208411_comment'></div>皇太后以无我之慈，至明之照，既已察臣之忠矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1208411_comment'></div>臣今日之言，必是亦蒙照察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1208411_comment'></div>今虽未察，终无不察之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1208411_comment'></div>臣虽远去朝廷，仰赖慈庇，纵未牵复，于臣无损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1208411_comment'></div>臣所望者，当以流窜蔡京为急，不当以移臣差遣为先也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1208411_comment'></div>盖恐京在朝廷，则烦言日进；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1208411_comment'></div>烦言日进，则圣虑日劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1208411_comment'></div>朝廷虽严示威刑，而天下公议，终不可遏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1208411_comment'></div>盖公议若必以威势夺之，则人心离矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1208411_comment'></div>人心既离，则主势孤弱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1208411_comment'></div>主势孤弱，则外陵内侮，何所不至！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1208411_comment'></div>非所以奉承宗庙，而慰安东朝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1208411_comment'></div>然则蔡京之所谓孝者，果天子之孝乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1208411_comment'></div>愿陛下勿爱一京，而切为国家之虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1208411_comment'></div>臣愚不胜惓惓爱君忧国之心，惟陛下裁赦，幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_77_1208411_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208419' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208419' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208419?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论允执厥中奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208419")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208419_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208419'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208419'>臣闻尧曰：「咨尔舜，天之历数在尔躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208419_comment'></div>允执厥中，四海困穷，天禄永终」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208419_comment'></div>舜亦以命禹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208419_comment'></div>盖历数在躬，则有天命也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208419_comment'></div>允执厥中，则尽人事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208419_comment'></div>天人两得，则四海不穷，而天禄永固矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208419_comment'></div>尧之所以命舜，舜之所以命禹者如是，则祖宗之所以命陛下者亦可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208419_comment'></div>陛下奄有神器，以天之历数在圣躬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208419_comment'></div>今所以保四海而固天禄者，在允执厥中以奉天而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208419_comment'></div>无过不及之谓中，不高不下之谓中，不左不右之谓中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208419_comment'></div>如天之有北辰，众星之所拱也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208419_comment'></div>如地之有洛邑，道里之所均也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208419_comment'></div>如五行之有土，万物之所以生也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208419_comment'></div>如五脏之有胃，百骸之所以立也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208419_comment'></div>知其理而言之者，儒生之所能也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208419_comment'></div>体其道而行之，则非圣人不能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208419_comment'></div>列子论出石入火之事，以谓仲尼能之而能不为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208419_comment'></div>能高而不为高，可谓中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208419_comment'></div>故六经之道高，而不可不中者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208419_comment'></div>岂唯六经为然哉，老子之道可谓高矣，然以百姓心为心，则取域中之大焉，有去甚之说焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208419_comment'></div>老尚如此，况吾儒乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208419_comment'></div>显诸仁，藏诸用，一弛一张，而不失乎中者，然后足以经世也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208419_comment'></div>今天下学者求治道于庄老，而于汉唐之事皆不取焉，失于高矣，故不中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208419_comment'></div>又天下之士，一南一北，彼用则此废，此用则彼废，失于偏矣，故不中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208419_comment'></div>不中，则如车轮无毂，不能转物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208419_comment'></div>不能转，则为物所转，此自然之理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208419_comment'></div>尧曰四句，自有次叙，故历数在躬，则当允执厥中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208419_comment'></div>允执厥中，然后永保天禄。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1208419_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208429' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208429' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208429?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进故事奏<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208429")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208429_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208429'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208429'>仁宗听讲《诗》，至《匪风》曰「谁能烹鱼，溉之釜鬵」，仁宗曰：「老子谓治大国若烹小鲜，其义类此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208429_comment'></div>然则古人之兴喻，其情岂相远也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208429_comment'></div>侍读丁度对曰：「烹鱼烦则碎，治民烦则散，非圣学之深，何以见古人求治之意乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208429_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1208429'>臣按古之圣君，适当大有为之时者，或创业，或革弊，不免有所烦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208429_comment'></div>仁祖以清净无为之道，持盈守成，四十二年，终始如一，盖得烹鲜之说而躬行之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208429_comment'></div>臣故曰，汉文之术出于老子，而仁祖之治多似汉文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208429_comment'></div>神考谓汉文吾无间然，则绍述仁祖之意可知也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1208429_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208420' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208420' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208420?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞悯恤山陵人夫奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208420")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208420_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208420'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208420'>臣闻唐穆宗山陵时，久雨时寒，役人饥冻颇甚，至有持锸抱彗而死者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208420_comment'></div>敬宗悯之，于是治路人夫各赐之绢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208420_comment'></div>臣谓绢者有限之物，岂得人人而与之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208420_comment'></div>兼诸色应奉之人例皆劳苦，所可矜者非特治路人夫而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208420_comment'></div>国家自裕陵以前，大事既毕之后，即降德音下两京等处，凡干应奉之人悉蒙恩恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208420_comment'></div>惠而不费，非赐绢之比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208420_comment'></div>乃者泰陵应奉之人，缘雨水异常，州县督责甚于他时，所以叙其情而悯其劳者亦宜加厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208420_comment'></div>惟陛下留意，幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1208420_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208423' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208423' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208423?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论用人惟己奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208423")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208423_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208423'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208423'>臣闻用人惟己，亦成汤之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208423_comment'></div>臣尝谓，立贤无方，则朝廷不偏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208423_comment'></div>用人惟己，则臣下无党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208423_comment'></div>为君之难，在此两者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208423_comment'></div>成汤所以能由此道而为后王之师者，始于执中而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208423_comment'></div>中则不偏，中则无党，无偏无党，王道荡荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208423_comment'></div>神考熙宁之初，立贤有方，用人惟安石；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208423_comment'></div>熙宁之末，立贤无方，用人惟己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208423_comment'></div>一弛一张，得文武之道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208423_comment'></div>有始有卒，见圣人之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208423_comment'></div>此陛下今日之所当法也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1208423_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208421' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208421' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208421?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞罢温益给事中奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208421")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208421_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208421'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208421'>右，臣闻汉高祖即位之初，所先封者皆故旧亲爱之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208421_comment'></div>用张良之言，急封雍齿，于是群臣人人有自坚之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208421_comment'></div>唐太宗即位之初，秦府旧人未迁官者皆有咨怨，房乔以为请，而太宗答曰：「设官分职，以为民也，当择贤才而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208421_comment'></div>今不论其贤不肖，而直言怨嗟，岂为政之体乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208421_comment'></div>臣愚以谓张良之谏有益于高祖，房乔之请无补于太宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208421_comment'></div>此二君者，一则有听谏之明，一则有察言之公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208421_comment'></div>故当即政之初，不失用人之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208421_comment'></div>此汉唐既往之善，初政之所当稽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208421_comment'></div>臣伏闻太常少卿温益除给事中、兼侍读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208421_comment'></div>按益知潭州日，有新州羁管人邹浩道过本州，晚投僧寺，就宿寄食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208421_comment'></div>而益差本州兵马都监遣浩出门，续令走卒数辈逼浩登舟，使之冒风夜渡而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208421_comment'></div>浩以言事得罪，既经行遣，不知所过州军更缘何事催辱逼逐，使至于此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208421_comment'></div>又分司安置人范纯仁、刘奉世、韩川、吕希纯、吕陶皆在本路，并为益所侵困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208421_comment'></div>当时用事大臣以益为是，而天下公议以益为非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208421_comment'></div>今陛下召还邹浩，厚礼纯仁，而奉世之徒皆已叙复，所以合天下之公是非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208421_comment'></div>益之所为又已达于圣听，谓宜躬揽之初，正益之罪，而乃擢置侍从，处之经筵，付以封駮之任，非缘端府旧僚，何以致此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208421_comment'></div>臣愿陛下用尧舜大公之法，稽汉唐既往之事，罢益新除，黜之于外，使天下皆知陛下不以故旧之私恩而废天下之公议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208421_comment'></div>如是，则一除之失，何足以累圣政；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208421_comment'></div>而不吝之明，适足以新盛德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208421_comment'></div>臣不胜惓惓爱君之忠，惟陛下加听，幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1208421_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208426' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208426' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208426?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论思患预防奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208426")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208426_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208426'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208426'>臣闻《易》曰：「穷则变，变则通，通则久」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208426_comment'></div>是故天下之事，穷则必变，变而后通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208426_comment'></div>人不通之，天必自变，此必然之理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208426_comment'></div>乃者用事之臣以私灭公，势力已穷，犹不悔悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208426_comment'></div>先帝有欲变之心，而左右无将顺之臣，焦劳忧悔，奄弃天下，摧伤痛恨，海内所同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208426_comment'></div>陛下受天眷命，增光前烈，慈孝之治，欣然以和，未有更张，人心已服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208426_comment'></div>朝廷之宽大可必，生民之休息有期，讴歌所归，鼓舞相庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208426_comment'></div>然而臣愚以谓既往之迹无足追论，未来之事所可深虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208426_comment'></div>今西边虽已罢兵，然正是大军之后，假使诸路丰熟，此方必有凶年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208426_comment'></div>民物凋残，加以水旱，人不饱暖，何事不生？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208426_comment'></div>又况河北居民流亡太半，仓廪匮竭，城壁不完，恃北虏之不来，我因循而无备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208426_comment'></div>老胡耄矣，馀日几何，其孙好杀，理必生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208426_comment'></div>朝廷自侍从而上，多是东南之人，西北事宜，久不诹访。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208426_comment'></div>虽云造作边事不在今日，然恐意外之变适出此时，若不先事而图，恐有后时之悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208426_comment'></div>可防之患，安得不思，思而防之，又有大于此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208426_comment'></div>太宗谓侍臣曰：「外忧不过边事，皆可预防；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208426_comment'></div>唯奸邪无状，若为内患，深可惧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208426_comment'></div>帝王用心，常须慎此」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208426_comment'></div>呜呼，太宗之训可谓明矣，有状者以为可防，无迹者以为可惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208426_comment'></div>今日之事，盖亦有无迹而可惧者矣，朋党是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208426_comment'></div>唐宪宗问李绛曰：「人言外间朋党太盛，何也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208426_comment'></div>李绛对曰：「朋党言之则可恶，寻之则无迹」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208426_comment'></div>呜呼，人之为邪至于无迹可寻，岂不深可惧乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208426_comment'></div>臣以唐事考之，牛李二党皆党也，然而李德裕之党多君子，牛僧孺之党多小人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208426_comment'></div>何以知其然邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208426_comment'></div>德裕之徒忌克自任，不同己者则显然排斥，故其为党也有形而可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208426_comment'></div>僧孺之徒忌克自私，不同己者则闇然挤陷，故其为党也无迹而难寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208426_comment'></div>此二党者皆明主之罪人也，然彼善于此，不可不辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208426_comment'></div>故臣因论太宗圣训，而以无迹者为尤可惧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208426_comment'></div>方今大明既升，凤德在上，乃邪朋消散之始，是至治必成之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208426_comment'></div>然而成则有败，始则有终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1208426_comment'></div>老子曰：「人之从事，常于几成而败之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1208426_comment'></div>慎终如始，则无败事矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1208426_comment'></div>故臣有思患预防之说。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1208426_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208427' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208427' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208427?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞六朝尚书依旧独员上殿劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208427")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208427_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208427'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208427'>臣伏睹近降圣旨，六曹尚书独员上殿，及文臣带一路兵钤及监司职任者，朝辞日并须上殿指挥更不施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208427_comment'></div>臣窃惟尚书之职，其选甚高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208427_comment'></div>自行官制以来，多自此官而除执政，朝廷所以待之可谓厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208427_comment'></div>元丰之末，始有不得独员上殿之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208427_comment'></div>绍圣之初，寻即改正，所以示优礼而去疑贰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208427_comment'></div>今复罢此指挥，其故何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208427_comment'></div>监司当一路之寄，兵钤受方面之托，以人主之好恶达于远方，不使一对清光，何由面禀圣训？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208427_comment'></div>况先朝之法行之已久，别无大害，不必轻改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208427_comment'></div>臣今欲乞六曹尚书许独员上殿，及文臣带一路兵钤及监司职任者，朝辞日并须上殿，皆依旧施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1208427_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208402' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208402' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208402?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论向宗良兄弟交通宾客奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208402")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208402_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208402'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208402'>臣闻知几而预戒，则君无过举；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208402_comment'></div>先事而早谏，则臣无智名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208402_comment'></div>君明臣良，上下两得，治道所以隆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208402_comment'></div>臣以驽散之才，冒处言职，适遭明圣之主，窃慕良臣之义，事有临机不当默者，安可有待而不早言乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208402_comment'></div>宋有天下一百四十一年矣，太平之久，尧、舜三代，乃至汉唐，皆不及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208402_comment'></div>譬如安乐之人，年过百岁，尤当兢兢畏慎，护养元气，无使疾患乘间而入，则愈老愈健，永保康宁之福矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208402_comment'></div>祖宗以圣继圣，古无有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208402_comment'></div>母后继有圣德，亦古无有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208402_comment'></div>天覆地载，一健一顺，万物生成，各遂其性，至神考而治道益隆，至皇太后而家道益光，可谓盛之极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208402_comment'></div>盛必有衰，安可不预戒乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208402_comment'></div>汉之衰也，以外家太盛，人不敢言，以至亡国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208402_comment'></div>陛下守祖宗之成法，监衰汉之覆辙，宋德方隆，内外无患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208402_comment'></div>然以臣所闻，宜预戒者有一事焉，恐陛下未知也，恐皇太后未知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208402_comment'></div>向宗良兄弟，交通宾客，漏泄机密，陛下知乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208402_comment'></div>皇太后知乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208402_comment'></div>皇太后功德隆备，格于皇天，陛下极天下养，未足以报，惟使我宋固万年不拔之基，外家享与国无疆之福，夫然后足以为报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208402_comment'></div>汉唐母后称制，有至终身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208402_comment'></div>或欲威福之柄，久出于己；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208402_comment'></div>或因左右之请，贪恋权势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208402_comment'></div>惟我皇太后恬寂足以全威福，严明足以戢左右，不待祔庙，果于还政，事光前古，名垂后世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208402_comment'></div>陛下所以报皇太后者宜如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208402_comment'></div>臣恐假借外家，不足以为报也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208402_comment'></div>乃者还政以前，陛下欲除向宗良等开府仪同三司，将锁学士院矣，而皇太后诏寝此命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208402_comment'></div>中外传闻，咨嗟叹仰，知皇太后以撝谦为德，而陛下以养志为孝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208402_comment'></div>汉章帝欲加恩三舅，马后曰：「吾观富贵之家，禄位重叠，犹再实之木，其根必伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208402_comment'></div>何必营外家之封，违慈母之拳拳？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208402_comment'></div>至孝之行，安亲为主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208402_comment'></div>此吾家之事，故得专之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208402_comment'></div>吾当含饴弄孙，不能复关政矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208402_comment'></div>于是章帝不封其舅<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208402_comment'></div>今皇太后盛德全备，与天同功，非马后之比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1208402_comment'></div>臣之所言，但欲有补于外家而已，想亦皇太后之所乐闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1208402_comment'></div>若不达圣母之心，而自为猜嫌之虑，当言不言，臣所不忍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1208402_comment'></div>臣谓马后之所以诏其子，章帝之所以顺其亲，内慈外孝，两得之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1208402_comment'></div>陛下及皇太后前日之事，撝谦养志，正与此同，天下之所以服也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1208402_comment'></div>汉哀帝之初，急封诸舅，孔光谏曰：「天下者，陛下之家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1208402_comment'></div>肺腑何患不富贵？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1208402_comment'></div>不宜仓猝若是，其不久长矣」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1208402_comment'></div>帝以逼于傅太后，不能从也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1208402_comment'></div>今皇太后诏寝成命，不待孔光之言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1208402_comment'></div>陛下恭禀慈训，遂无仓猝之举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1208402_comment'></div>此乃前古难行之事，于今见之，皇太后之圣德可胜言乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1208402_comment'></div>陛下所以报皇太后者宜如何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1208402_comment'></div>臣恐假借外家，不足以为报也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1208402_comment'></div>陛下虽受天眷命，历数在躬，然而力摧异议，独定大策者，皇太后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1208402_comment'></div>盖有功于陛下者，天及皇太后而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1208402_comment'></div>天道公而不私，陛下之所以报天者宜如何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1208402_comment'></div>皇太后为而不恃，功成不居，陛下之所以报皇太后者宜如何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1208402_comment'></div>陛下以道制情，无一毫之私，则可以服人之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1208402_comment'></div>服人之心，则可以得天之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1208402_comment'></div>得天之心，则可以合皇太后之意矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1208402_comment'></div>神考之所以报慈圣者，用此道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1208402_comment'></div>治平之末，韩琦为相，中外协心，定策为易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1208402_comment'></div>前日之事，章惇秉政，首唱异议，定策为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1208402_comment'></div>然则皇太后之功，比之慈圣，又为光矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1208402_comment'></div>陛下之所以报皇太后者宜如何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1208402_comment'></div>唐之衰也，天以定策之功付于矜伐之臣，于是责报不已，而有「负心门生」之语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1208402_comment'></div>主道之强弱，可见于此矣<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1208402_comment'></div>今者功出圣母，国本既正，唯陛下永思所以图报而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1208402_comment'></div>大公之报，报之上也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1208402_comment'></div>假借外家，岂足以为报乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1208402_comment'></div>宗良兄弟依倚国恩，凭藉慈荫，夸有目前之荣盛，不念倚伏之可畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1208402_comment'></div>所与游者，连及侍从，希宠之士，愿出其门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1208402_comment'></div>裴彦臣无甚干才，但能交通内外，漏泄机密<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>，遂使物议籍籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1208402_comment'></div>或者以谓万机之事，黜陟差除，皇太后至今与也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1208402_comment'></div>良由中外关通，未有禁戒，故好事之人得以溢传耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1208402_comment'></div>若非皇太后明谕圣意，严加约束，则籍籍之口，未易塞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1208402_comment'></div>仁宗笃于舅家，尤以李玮为贤，诏玮举官为将领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1208402_comment'></div>玮言家有宾客之禁，无以知士人之贤否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1208402_comment'></div>仁宗特许玮见宾客，而命日抄所见宾客名氏以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1208402_comment'></div>盖仁宗之所以保全外家者，委曲周旋，至于如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1208402_comment'></div>神宗敬厚曹佾，加以王爵，然而佾口不敢荐一人，佾门不敢接一人，不过以自娱乐而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1208402_comment'></div>神考所以厚佾而无厌者，以其得外戚之体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1208402_comment'></div>宣仁圣烈皇后戒训外家，尤为切至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1208402_comment'></div>绍圣时利口之祸，几及门户，然而高氏之族终获免者，则亦宣仁训戒之明效也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1208402_comment'></div>皇太后功德之大，光于前人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1208402_comment'></div>念保持之艰，为无疆之虑，事戒其渐，正在今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1208402_comment'></div>《老子》曰：「为之其未有也，治之其未乱也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1208402_comment'></div>凡未有之事，今虽无之，后或渐有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1208402_comment'></div>既有而后图，不如未有而先戒之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1208402_comment'></div>汉之马廖，章帝之舅也，倾身交结，冠盖之士争趋赴之，遂至于私赡三辅，第五伦之所言者是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1208402_comment'></div>今虽未有此事，安可以不戒其渐乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1208402_comment'></div>王氏依东宫之尊，假甥舅之亲以为威重，内外要官皆出其门，推誉者登进，忤恨者诛伤，刘向之所言者是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1208402_comment'></div>今虽未有此事，安可以不戒其渐乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1208402_comment'></div>杜钦、谷永自托于外戚，专攻人主之身，而无一言敢及王凤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1208402_comment'></div>遇有灾变，则反推天异，归之他人，以为外戚之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1208402_comment'></div>怀二心之士，如杜钦、谷永者，何代无之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1208402_comment'></div>今虽未有此事，安可以不戒其渐乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1208402_comment'></div>成帝之时，外家子弟，据势满朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1208402_comment'></div>成帝欲以刘歆为中常侍，临欲拜官，而左右奏曰：「未白大将军，不肯奉诏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1208402_comment'></div>帝虽坚执，终不能夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1208402_comment'></div>由是朝廷之事，只由外家，不由成帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1208402_comment'></div>今虽未有此事，安可不戒其渐乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1208402_comment'></div>王音、王根，奢僭不法，天子怒之，于是兄弟欲自黥劓以谢太后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1208402_comment'></div>封侯之日，黄雾四塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1208402_comment'></div>谏大夫杨兴等以王氏为言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1208402_comment'></div>于是大将军惶惧，乞骸辞职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1208402_comment'></div>然而外家强盛，故人主之威终不得行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1208402_comment'></div>今虽未有此事，安可以不戒其渐乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1208402_comment'></div>神考有言曰：「荒坠颠危，可见前车之失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1208402_comment'></div>乱贼奸宄，厥有履霜之渐」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1208402_comment'></div>臣愚以谓欲见前车之失，则往古之事不可以不考；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1208402_comment'></div>欲辨履霜之渐，则方今之事不可以不戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1208402_comment'></div>《老子》曰：「合抱之木，生于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_103_1208402", 1208402, "Clauses/310/Comments/0")'>毫末</span>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1208402_comment'></div>九层之台，起于累土」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1208402_comment'></div>事之有渐者，无不然也<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1208402_comment'></div>汉之王商、王章，皆当时之贤臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1208402_comment'></div>因为王凤所恶，一则死于暗昧之过，一则死于缧绁之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1208402_comment'></div>当此之时，外家之势已如合抱之木、九层之台，岂一手之所能拔，岂一锸之所能平哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1208402_comment'></div>商等区区可怜，而谏诤后时，戒之不早，何益于事！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1208402_comment'></div>今臣所论，乃在于累土、<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_110_1208402", 1208402, "Clauses/329/Comments/1")'>毫末</span>之初，遏萌杜渐，何难之有！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1208402_comment'></div>在陛下从容求皇太后一言之诏而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1208402_comment'></div>自古戚里侵权，便为衰世之象；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1208402_comment'></div>外家干政，即是亡国之本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1208402_comment'></div>亦如州县之政，只要权出于一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1208402_comment'></div>若使守令人家子弟亲戚交通宾客，关节无禁，如此则奸人鼓舞，良民咨嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1208402_comment'></div>此陛下及皇太后之所不取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1208402_comment'></div>以小喻大，有以异乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1208402_comment'></div>臣愿陛下采刍荛之言，念老子之说，遵神考之训，合太母之心，以臣此疏达于慈闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1208402_comment'></div>若蒙皇太后察臣愚直，以慈爱之，则自今日已往，忧国忘身之士，皆欲竭忠自效，而无所畏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1208402_comment'></div>臣下尽乐告之忠，朝廷有不讳之善，好察如虞舜，不吝如成汤<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑸</sup>，圣德日跻，治道日隆，我宋固万年不拔之基，外家享与国无疆之福，岂特贱臣一身之幸乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1208402_comment'></div>如其不然，则臣有僭易妄言之罪，罢黜投窜，理不可逃，在陛下命之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1208402_comment'></div>臣以孤寒远贱之迹，误蒙陛下过有拔擢，责臣不轻，眷臣方厚，臣是以及时而言，先事而谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1208402_comment'></div>岂敢以身之不肖而自废其所当言乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1208402_comment'></div>孔子曰：「君子不以言<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_124_1208402", 1208402, "Clauses/379/Comments/1")'>举人</span>，不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_124_1208402", 1208402, "Clauses/380/Comments/1")'>以人废言</span>」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1208402_comment'></div>臣虽不肖，而区区之言，有益于朝廷，有补于外家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1208402_comment'></div>若不以臣之不肖而取之，则忠言由此而并进；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1208402_comment'></div>若以臣之不肖而废臣之言，则谄言由此而交人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1208402_comment'></div>听言，治之基也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1208402_comment'></div>信谄，乱之本也<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑹</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1208402_comment'></div>国家治乱之机在此一举，臣一身蝼蚁之命，安危生死，岂足道哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1208402_comment'></div>臣不胜惶惧待罪之至。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_131_1208402'></div><div id='poem_sentence_131_1208402_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1208402'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_1208402_0'>⑴ 〔贴黄〕马后不复关政之言，恻怛如此，可谓贤矣。然后以兄弟干政，后世议焉。唐之长孙皇后曰：「汉之马后，不能检抑外家，使预政事，乃戒其车马之侈，此所谓开本源而恤末事也。」是以太宗问后政事，后不欲言，再三要之，终不肯对，盖以马后为戒也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_57_1208402_0'>⑵ 〔贴黄〕唐宦者杨复恭策立昭宗，后稍恣横，责报不已，昭宗后厌之，因令致仕。遂与其兄子守亮书曰：「吾披荆榛立寿王为天子。既有天下，遂废定策国老，奈负心门生何！」门生，谓昭宗也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_63_1208402_0'>⑶ 〔贴黄〕臣闻绍圣之初，裴彦臣管干造慈云寺，因妇人阿王赴户部及御史台理会地界。后来并此一寺，屡曾迁徙，竟不成就。臣切恨此也。皇太后为追荐爱主，所以施财造寺，此寺既不成就，而郝随之徒因缘恣横，敢慢东朝，外人皆有不平之心，所恨哲宗不知耳。当时户部及御史台官司，有以彦臣为是者，有以彦臣为非者。是非自有公议。以臣观之，只因彦臣干当不了，以致生事。臣故曰：彦臣无甚干才也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_105_1208402_0'>⑷ 〔贴黄〕王凤擅权，以王商不附己，使人上书极言，诋毁商暗昧之过。商发病呕血死。王章不亲附王凤，乃奏封事，言日食之咎，皆凤擅权蔽主之过。天子感悟纳之，谓章曰：「微章直言，不闻社稷计。且惟贤知贤，君试为予求所以自辅者。」于是章荐冯野王。王音切知其语，以告大将军凤。凤用杜钦计，称病乞骸。太后闻之，为垂涕不御食。成帝乃优诏报凤，强起之，于是凤视事。后下章吏，廷尉致其大逆罪。章竟死狱中，妻子徙合浦。自是公卿见凤侧目而视。冯野王竟免官。众庶多冤王商议朝政者。杜钦复为凤画策，诏求直言极谏，以救前过。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_120_1208402_0'>⑸ 〔贴黄〕《中庸》曰：「好察迩言。」舜之事也。《诗》曰：「唯迩言是听。」幽王之事也。此二者相去远矣，在分听察两字而已。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_129_1208402_0'>⑹ 〔贴黄〕古者忠信之士，语及外家，则谗谄之人必中伤之，指为离间，以激怒内外，然后奸谋秘计，无所不行。此计若行，则言者必危。言者既危，则天下之士以言为戒。如此则乱可必矣。臣故曰：信谄者乱之本也。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1208402_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年9月18日</a>　谪监扬州粮料院。陈瓘不知皇上责，复求翌日见上，閤门不许。瓘即以札子请进。作品：再论景灵西宫。<span class='inlineComment2'>（上批：“陈瓘累言皇太后尚与国事，其言多虚诞不根，可送吏部合入差遣。”谪监扬州粮料院。）</span><div id='poem_1208406' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208406' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208406?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再论修建景灵西宫劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208406")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208406_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208406'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208406'>臣昨具劄子，言修建景灵西宫有可议者五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208406_comment'></div>续具奏状，言祖宗神御与圣祖天兴殿皆列于天庙之次，不当迁徙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208406_comment'></div>续又具劄子，言真祖用道家之制，而参取阴阳之说，神考依礼经之旨，而不易左右之位，今一举而两失之，愿诏三省、枢密院及侍从台谏官重行审议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208406_comment'></div>未蒙施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208406_comment'></div>臣窃惟宗庙之祠不可轻易，祖宗之绪不宜茍改，而朝廷固执初议，臣不敢以为然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208406_comment'></div>《周礼义》曰：「位宗庙于人道之所向者，不死其亲之意也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208406_comment'></div>不死其亲虽公羊之旧说，而三经妙义乃神考之所以训天下者也，庙社之说安可破乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208406_comment'></div>今欲弃先儒之是说，违神考之圣训，专用私意，率改成绪，臣是以知其不然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208406_comment'></div>或者以谓，若东展旧基，则高头街之地必见侵掘，国之左臂不可侵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208406_comment'></div>夫天庙之说出于阴阳家，真宗用之，今尚不取，何独左臂之说为可据乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208406_comment'></div>况旧基之北有榷货务，移一务，则不动民居而得殿基矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208406_comment'></div>不欲侵掘，则因地形之高下，何为不可？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208406_comment'></div>释此可因之绪，而坚持难就之计，臣是以知其不然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208406_comment'></div>又或谓，以祖宗神御昔者或东或西，或南或北，随寺观之所在即置殿宇，岂有左右之拘乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208406_comment'></div>臣谓随处奉安，斯无定位，会而为一，必辨东西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208406_comment'></div>昔者散处之时，后或在南，帝或在北，今既会而为一，岂可以不分南北，而皆以因旧为说乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208406_comment'></div>臣是以知其不然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208406_comment'></div>夫此三不然者，皆不足以固守，然陛下所以不敢轻改前议者，谓神考素有修建西宫之意，蔡京亲闻先训，而《实录》备载其语，故不可以不恭依也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208406_comment'></div>陛下用史官亲闻之语，遵神考素定之意，以奉先之孝，述宗庙之事，臣下之所宜将顺，其有大于此乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208406_comment'></div>然而以臣观之，此乃蔡京矫诬神考之训，无足信者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208406_comment'></div>臣请以一事验之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208406_comment'></div>元丰中，神考于英宗治隆殿后留一殿之基，宣仁诏曰：「此以待未亡人也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208406_comment'></div>因逊此基为神考庙宫之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208406_comment'></div>宣仁之意，不欲多迁民居耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208406_comment'></div>而绍圣大臣因谓宣仁轻蔑神考，裁损庙制，于是重卜奉安之地，以极崇报之礼，今显承殿是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208406_comment'></div>方建修显承殿之时，蔡京正在朝廷，若神考之言审如《实录》所载，京于此时何不具以先训闻于哲宗？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208406_comment'></div>况当哲宗之时，京最用事，凡可以毁宣仁者无遗力矣，岂有宗庙重事，亲闻先训，可以證元祐之非，无大于此，而乃隐忍不言，复何待乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208406_comment'></div>臣是以验其为矫诬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208406_comment'></div>且绍圣之初，哲宗圣意本无适莫，章惇虽挟功自恣，然其初犹有兼取元祐之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208406_comment'></div>及京自成都而来，与其弟卞共毁宣仁，共欺哲宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208406_comment'></div>京之得售其说自役法始，从大改役法以后，事事无不大改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1208406_comment'></div>兄弟同朝，埙篪相和，无有一事不如其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1208406_comment'></div>当此之时，不以所闻神考圣训告于哲宗，至于今日，然后引所自书《实录》以为證验，唱为不经之论，而欲迁神考于西宫，其为矫诬，可谓明矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1208406_comment'></div>京以矫诬之笔，妄增《实录》之事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1208406_comment'></div>以矫诬之舌，伪造神考之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1208406_comment'></div>朝廷用矫诬之言而轻改宗庙，信矫诬之说而力沮言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1208406_comment'></div>臣恐自此以后，矫诬之人无复忌惮，矫诬之政不可复救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1208406_comment'></div>奸雄生心，四夷相贺，必始于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1208406_comment'></div>伏望圣慈出自睿断，正京矫诬之罪，明示贬窜，然后三省、枢密院及侍从、台谏官如臣所请，重行审议。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1208406_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年9月18日</a>　陈瓘不知皇上责，复求翌日见上，閤门不许。瓘即以札子请进。作品：论章惇罢相制所称国是。其三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（其三其四皆指陈蔡京罪恶，并明宣仁诬谤事。）</span>其四。<span class='inlineComment2'>（其三其四皆指陈蔡京罪恶，并明宣仁诬谤事。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年9月21日</a>　九月甲申，翰林学士曾肇言，陈瓘以一言对贬，当隐忍包容。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年9月24日</a>　诏新添差监扬州粮料院陈瓘知无为军，瓘于国门外露章辞免，并上章论蔡京，十月，蔡京出知永兴军。作品：论蔡京交结外戚。<div id='poem_1208411' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208411' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208411?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论蔡京交结外戚奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208411")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208411_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208411'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208411'>臣近为言事不根，谪授监扬州粮料院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208411_comment'></div>受告方得数日，便蒙改差知无为军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208411_comment'></div>闻命皇惑，唯知感涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208411_comment'></div>臣闻圣人之过也，如日月之食焉，人皆见之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208411_comment'></div>及其更也，人皆仰之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208411_comment'></div>朝廷以一时之怒，黜忠谏之臣，此如日月之食也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208411_comment'></div>今兹改命，可见圣人之心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208411_comment'></div>天下有识之人，谁不叹仰！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208411_comment'></div>岂独贱臣一身之私幸乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208411_comment'></div>臣虽上感圣恩，而未敢便受新命者，诚有说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208411_comment'></div>明道中，仁祖欲率群臣为皇太后上寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208411_comment'></div>范仲淹谏曰：「人主无北面之礼」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208411_comment'></div>明肃大怒，而仲淹得罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208411_comment'></div>元祐中，蔡确之贬，范纯仁以为不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208411_comment'></div>宣仁大怒，而纯仁得罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208411_comment'></div>此二臣者，可黜可逐，而尊主不贰之心，不可以威势夺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208411_comment'></div>方刘氏甚危之日，极力救护，却是仲淹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208411_comment'></div>以宣仁晚年，翻然远虑，复思纯仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208411_comment'></div>知忠言之有益于国家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208411_comment'></div>大抵忠臣之心，唯欲保全国体，为千万年久长之虑，岂忍使天下议论及于慈闱！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208411_comment'></div>今宗良等内外交通，迹状甚明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208411_comment'></div>蔡京交结之迹，天下所共知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208411_comment'></div>京作《向縡墓志》曰：「吾平生与士大夫游，无如承旨蔡公与我厚者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208411_comment'></div>京为从官，而与外戚相厚，书于碑刻，以自矜夸，如此之类，非止一事而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208411_comment'></div>又京与弟卞久在朝廷，同恶相济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208411_comment'></div>卞则出矣，京则牢不可拔，自谓执政可以决取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208411_comment'></div>人皆谓京因慈云寺得裴彦臣交结之助，外议讻讻，众所知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208411_comment'></div>京作《向宗良麻词》云：「元丰末命，尝有嘉言」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208411_comment'></div>嘉言若出于宗良，则大谤必归于宣仁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208411_comment'></div>京亦自谓，曾带开封府刽子，携剑入内，欲斩王圭，以沮宣仁怀异之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208411_comment'></div>京以禁中疑似之传，书于制命，扬于天庭，自谓与宗良皆社稷之功，而使宣仁负无穷之谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1208411_comment'></div>京之谄事外戚，不畏上天，一至如此，岂惟有害于朝廷，实亦无益于外家！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1208411_comment'></div>臣尽忠于陛下，尽忠于皇太后，所以言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1208411_comment'></div>皇太后圣德大功，冠绝今古，陛下承颜养志，方以大舜、武王为法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1208411_comment'></div>入修家人之礼，则恭顺无阙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1208411_comment'></div>出治朝廷之事，则威柄不分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1208411_comment'></div>大舜、武王之孝，何以加于此乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1208411_comment'></div>京所谓孝则不然，但欲陛下授柄于外家而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1208411_comment'></div>此蔡氏之利，非宗社之福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1208411_comment'></div>陛下以圣德嗣位，春秋方富，如汉文帝、宣帝即位之年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1208411_comment'></div>尽孝于东朝，励精于政事，独操大柄，足以有为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1208411_comment'></div>而京之所以胁持陛下者，原其用意，谓陛下未可以独为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1208411_comment'></div>哲宗躬揽之初，圣意本无适莫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1208411_comment'></div>章子厚虽挟功自恣，然其初犹有兼取元祐之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1208411_comment'></div>自京、卞首发邪论，盗攘国柄，凡有所请，必以继述为说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1208411_comment'></div>稍违其意，则欲以不忠之名加于上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1208411_comment'></div>假朝廷之诛赏，示私门之好恶，轻君误国，首尾八年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1208411_comment'></div>至于今日，狃于故态，又以此意胁持陛下，傅会继述之论，假托报功之说，密持离间之谋，伺察陛下，包藏祸心，若有所待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1208411_comment'></div>京之出言用意，谅无逃陛下之圣察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1208411_comment'></div>且陛下述神考之圣德，报太母之大功，岂独陛下之私心，是亦臣子之所愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1208411_comment'></div>合臣子之所愿，尽四海之欢心，然后陛下有庆，兆民赖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1208411_comment'></div>天子之孝，孰大于此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1208411_comment'></div>今京所赖，非兆民之所同赖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1208411_comment'></div>陛下一违京意，则京必以不孝之名责陛下矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1208411_comment'></div>陛下徇一京胁持之私名，而不畏天下至公之大义乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1208411_comment'></div>畏天下至公之大义，当流窜蔡京，以安国家而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1208411_comment'></div>臣前日之言不负天，不负陛下，不负皇太后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1208411_comment'></div>果蒙陛下移臣差遣，若非皇太后察臣之忠，陛下必不欲如此旨挥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1208411_comment'></div>然而京在朝廷，则家国未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1208411_comment'></div>臣虽移得差遣，有何安乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1208411_comment'></div>臣之不敢受命者，其说如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1208411_comment'></div>臣露章所言，未甚子细；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1208411_comment'></div>复以此章干渎圣听，所以尽惓惓之诚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1208411_comment'></div>皇太后以无我之慈，至明之照，既已察臣之忠矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1208411_comment'></div>臣今日之言，必是亦蒙照察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1208411_comment'></div>今虽未察，终无不察之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1208411_comment'></div>臣虽远去朝廷，仰赖慈庇，纵未牵复，于臣无损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1208411_comment'></div>臣所望者，当以流窜蔡京为急，不当以移臣差遣为先也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1208411_comment'></div>盖恐京在朝廷，则烦言日进；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1208411_comment'></div>烦言日进，则圣虑日劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1208411_comment'></div>朝廷虽严示威刑，而天下公议，终不可遏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1208411_comment'></div>盖公议若必以威势夺之，则人心离矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1208411_comment'></div>人心既离，则主势孤弱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1208411_comment'></div>主势孤弱，则外陵内侮，何所不至！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1208411_comment'></div>非所以奉承宗庙，而慰安东朝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1208411_comment'></div>然则蔡京之所谓孝者，果天子之孝乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1208411_comment'></div>愿陛下勿爱一京，而切为国家之虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1208411_comment'></div>臣愚不胜惓惓爱君忧国之心，惟陛下裁赦，幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_77_1208411_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='a624b393b0d8429cb82e2a97bc0f19b2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a624b393b0d8429cb82e2a97bc0f19b2");'><span id='a624b393b0d8429cb82e2a97bc0f19b2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>，45岁</div><div id='a624b393b0d8429cb82e2a97bc0f19b2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年3月17日</a>　三月戊寅，改为著作佐郎、实录院检讨官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年7月8日</a>　七月丁卯，迁右司员外郎兼权给事中，瓘力辞实录院检讨官，从之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年8月10日</a>　承议郎陈瓘等并降一官，以馅附柄臣，倾摇先烈，猖从宽之邪说，诬至正之典常也。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　与左司员外郎朱彦周谒左仆射曾布与都堂，以书责布，并以《日录辨》及国用须知纳布而出。作品：进日录辨奏状。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷2783。）</span>进国用须知札子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷2783。）</span><div id='poem_1208415' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208415' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208415?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进日录辨奏状<span class='inlineComment2'>（建中靖国元年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年8月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208415")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208415_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208415'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208415'>臣瓘去年五月十八日对紫宸殿，奏劄子云：「臣闻王安石《日录》七十馀卷具载熙宁中奏对议论之语，此乃人臣私录之书，非朝廷之典也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208415_comment'></div>自绍圣再修《神考实录》，史官请以此书降付史院，凡《日录》、《政记》、《神宗御集》之所不载者，往往专据此书追议刑赏，夺宗庙之美以归臣下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208415_comment'></div>故臣愿诏史官别行删修，以成一代不刊之典」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208415_comment'></div>其日蒙批付三省，后不闻施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208415_comment'></div>盖绍圣史官请以《日录》降付史院者，今为宰相故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208415_comment'></div>臣位下人微，轻议大典，诚以宗庙至重，义不敢默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208415_comment'></div>盖惟神宗皇帝体道用极，宪天有为，自得师臣，授以政柄，虽尹暨汤，咸有一德，无以复异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208415_comment'></div>而嘉谋嘉猷，实出我后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208415_comment'></div>以言乎经术，则微言奥义，皆自得之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208415_comment'></div>以言乎政事，则改法就功，取成于心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208415_comment'></div>是则神考之独志，而安石之所以归美者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208415_comment'></div>用事之臣闇于此理，托奉宗庙，独尊安石，假绍述于诏令，寓好恶于刑赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208415_comment'></div>至于纂记私言，如嗣考事，遂使密赞之语宣扬于外，而一朝大典，祖述故事，但专美于人臣，不归德于我后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208415_comment'></div>淩压宗庙，以植其私，事之乖谬，莫大于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208415_comment'></div>岂惟负神考在天之灵，抑亦失安石事君之意，臣所以惓惓而不能已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208415_comment'></div>因以所见，撰成《日录辨》一篇，具状奏闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1208415_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208414' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208414' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208414?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进国用须知劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（建中靖国元年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208414")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208414_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208414'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208414'>臣伏见仁祖之时，臣寮上言曰：「周制冢宰制国用，唐宰相兼盐铁转运使，或判户部，或判度支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208414_comment'></div>然则宰相制国用，从古然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208414_comment'></div>今中书主民，枢密主兵，三司主财，各不相知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208414_comment'></div>故财已匮而枢密院益兵不已，民已困而三司取财不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208414_comment'></div>中书视民之困，而不知使枢密院减兵、三司减财以救民困者，制国用之职不在中书故也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208414_comment'></div>臣谓当仁祖之时，官制未立，自元丰以来，制国用之职在三省矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208414_comment'></div>户部右曹之所掌，乃天下财用之根本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208414_comment'></div>神考理财之政，所以法先王而虑万世，元祐之臣虽有纷更，然天下所积财物，朝廷亦不尽取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208414_comment'></div>今则一年之间，连下五敕，凡提举司所积钱取之殆尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208414_comment'></div>竭天下根本之财，坏神考理财之政，继志述事，岂宜然哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208414_comment'></div>今具五次朝旨下项。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208414_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1208414'>一、元符三年九月八日敕：「府界诸路见管坊场钱，除本路一年合支数外，将剩数更留一半准备支用，馀一半特令起发上京，应副朝廷支用」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208414_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1208414'>一、元符三年十一月十九日敕：「府界诸路见管常平役钱，除本路一年合支数外，将剩数更留一半准备支用，馀一半特令起发上京，应副朝廷支用」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208414_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1208414'>一、建中靖国元年二月二十三日敕：「诸路提举司将见在抵当息钱并起发上京，应副朝廷支用」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208414_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1208414'>一、建中靖国元年三月初一日敕：「诸路提举司将见在量添酒钱，依抵当息钱已得旨挥施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208414_comment'></div>今后支使不尽钱数，并封桩，准备朝廷支用」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208414_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1208414'>一、建中靖国元年三月初二日敕：「府界诸路提举司所管钱物，除依旨挥起发及除留出本年合支散外，馀剩更留一半，钱数不多，深属阙少籴本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208414_comment'></div>今于元祐年中所纳助役钱内拨一半充常平籴本，馀一半许榷货务召人入便，或计置起发上京，兑那往三路添助常平籴本」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208414_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1208414'>臣切惟神考立法之意，取民之财，还以助民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208414_comment'></div>故天下诸路，州州县县各有蓄积，将以待非常之用，不使有偏乏之处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208414_comment'></div>故右曹钱物不得与别司交杂，违条辄用者徒二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208414_comment'></div>自元丰七年以常平等积剩财物补助边费，岁取二百万缗为额，只以三年为期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208414_comment'></div>盖不欲多费天下民财以资边用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208414_comment'></div>神考爱民之虑，可谓深矣远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208414_comment'></div>今当绍述此意，岂宜取三十年间根本蓄藏之物，一切大违成宪，而偏用之于一方乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208414_comment'></div>且上件五项所取之类，以天下计之，万数不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208414_comment'></div>于此类内，河东、陕西、京西三路之拨与提刑司者其数几何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208414_comment'></div>河北路交拨与措置籴买司者其数几何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208414_comment'></div>川陕西路具桩管数目关邻路召人入便，及与茶马司对数交兑者其数几何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208414_comment'></div>臣谓凡此八路，那移兑拨，皆主于边费而已，自馀路分起发入京西飞于塞下者，又不知其几何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208414_comment'></div>然则天下蓄积之物，皆运之于边矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1208414_comment'></div>若使一劳而久佚，暂费而永宁，则三十年积之而一日用之，犹足以济一时之权，成不得已之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1208414_comment'></div>今则不然，但剔割诸路以补一方之疮痍而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1208414_comment'></div>臣恐一方疮痍补之未合，而天下乏财之患有不可深言者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1208414_comment'></div>臣生长南方，不能周知四境之事，且为东南之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1208414_comment'></div>西边财用匮竭，则供亿调度必取诸东南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1208414_comment'></div>东南积剩之物，今于无事之时，既巧取而偏用之矣，或有东南意外不庭之患，又将取之于何地乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1208414_comment'></div>臣切考唐武德以后，开拓边境，地连西域，置都督，列州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1208414_comment'></div>开元中置节度以统之，军城戍逻，万里相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1208414_comment'></div>然而当此之时，糗粮出于屯田，马牛出于监牧，戍卒缯布取足于山东而已，未尝罄天下之积以从事于一方也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1208414_comment'></div>今五敕之所取，非岁岁常有之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1208414_comment'></div>方主议臣充位之时，赖此纾目前之急；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1208414_comment'></div>为庙堂久远之虑，当如之何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1208414_comment'></div>制国用者既不恤此，议弃地者又执偏见，不询众庶之论，不尽边臣之说，各以私意自复其言，因循相仍，驯致大患，纵以阙乏为忧，不过请行鬻爵之类耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1208414_comment'></div>神考创法比隆于三代，彼中世之陋法，如鬻爵之类，乃熙宁初议之所不取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1208414_comment'></div>当时条例司臣寮参议论者，今为辅相，忍不为陛下一言之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1208414_comment'></div>又况神考自有为之初，以至法度之成，忧勤不倦，非一日之积也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1208414_comment'></div>所以建子孙万世之业，为四海无疆之虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1208414_comment'></div>何意今日继述先绪，乃复遽取中世之陋法而行之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1208414_comment'></div>使财用有馀，则朝廷议论自不至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1208414_comment'></div>然则神考十九年焦劳之虑，特为今日目前之费尔，岂不痛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1208414_comment'></div>又闻献议之臣欲裁损州郡供给，减削吏人请受，以佐国用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1208414_comment'></div>枢密院减罢陕西诸路准备官员数以节冗费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1208414_comment'></div>此不得已之计，非无毫发之助也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1208414_comment'></div>然使神考理财之政不为庙堂所坏，则臣寮议论亦不至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1208414_comment'></div>此等不得已之事，不免渐渐为之，则算间架，除钱陌，贷富人钱谷，卖御史告身之类，安保其不渐为也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1208414_comment'></div>主议大臣既去之后，设有此事，则其敛谤欲使何人当之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1208414_comment'></div>故凡户部不得已之下策，皆非神考大有为之初意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1208414_comment'></div>渐用不得已之策，顿改大有为之意，名曰「建中」而偏为过甚之举，名曰「继述」而大违神考之绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1208414_comment'></div>甚矣，其可痛也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1208414_comment'></div>陛下嗣位之初，肆赦天下，大弛逋欠，此乃真宗之所尝行，而神考之所欲为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1208414_comment'></div>绍圣役法有「一倍三料」之文，神考素意，欲候岁久积多则时一弛之，所以远继成周驭民之法，而俯取汉文弛租之政，以悦斯民，以召和气，以为后嗣之式也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1208414_comment'></div>夫上之所弛者其数既多，则下之所获者不为侥倖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1208414_comment'></div>《周官》「八则」，所谓予以驭其幸者，虽非日行之常事，是乃驭民之美意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1208414_comment'></div>陛下式祖宗而行之，可谓得继述之义，而人臣之所宜将顺者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1208414_comment'></div>然方国用匮乏之时，而所弛之物其数太多，故所谓倾天下之财而使无孑遗者，言者之所当虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1208414_comment'></div>然赦敕之所放，陛下所以广恩惠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1208414_comment'></div>五敕之所取，大臣所以备边乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1208414_comment'></div>广恩惠以收人心，有益之事也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1208414_comment'></div>因边费而坏成法，无益之举也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1208414_comment'></div>又赦敕所放，其数止于二千馀万；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1208414_comment'></div>五敕所取，其数不知其几万万也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1208414_comment'></div>陛下为有益之事以法祖宗，其数又少，方乏财之时，尚不可以不言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1208414_comment'></div>大臣为无益之举以坏先宪，其数甚多，方乏财之时，安可以不虑乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1208414_comment'></div>切惟神考承祖宗久安之绪，熙宁之初，国用匮乏，而理财之政未修也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1208414_comment'></div>王安石曰，有天下者岂以乏财为患哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1208414_comment'></div>于是讲理财之法，立天下之政，缉熙增损十有馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1208414_comment'></div>至于元丰之间，法度成就，然后州州县县皆有蓄积，天下无偏乏之处，将以待非常之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1208414_comment'></div>则所谓有天下者不以乏财为患，信不诬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1208414_comment'></div>今则不然，耗根本之财，坏已成之法，虽西边用度目前不乏，而天下方匮乏，患将由此而作矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1208414_comment'></div>盖神考为子孙万世之虑，故政事既立，而天下无乏财之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1208414_comment'></div>今日坏神考之法，则天下之患，必自乏财而生，此必然之理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1208414_comment'></div>且自祖宗以来，天下诸路转运司或有非常之用，必须干告朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1208414_comment'></div>既在经费之外，于理自合应副，然自熙宁以前，常患无可应副者，以理财之政未修故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1208414_comment'></div>由元丰以来，根本蓄积之财，州州县县聚如江海，法防坚固，内外充溢，转运司经费之外，设有干求，以此应副，不患不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1208414_comment'></div>然而神考爱惜民财，谨守交杂之法，转运司虽有干求，亦不轻与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1208414_comment'></div>故当时转运使刘攽之徒妄有乞贷者，皆被谪罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1208414_comment'></div>今则边方用度百倍于昔，转运司匮乏迫窘异于平时，虽有乞贷，理合应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1208414_comment'></div>然朝廷于其所请，例皆峻拒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1208414_comment'></div>朝廷岂为爱惜民财，谨交杂之法乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1208414_comment'></div>良以乏财而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1208414_comment'></div>诸路误以乏财废事，为转运使者，安肯受无名之谪乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1208414_comment'></div>夫州州县县蓄积之物，一年之内皆以五敕取之，而尚以乏财为患，可不虑哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1208414_comment'></div>臣愿陛下诏宰臣制国用，修户部右曹之政，明提举官覆奏之法，委官选吏，会计五敕所起都数若干，已到若干，未到若干；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1208414_comment'></div>自馀八路那移兑拨以充边用者若干；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1208414_comment'></div>陕西、河东边费，除系本路钱物及朝廷以钱应副外，已用五敕所及外，应支五敕所起者，其数各若干；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1208414_comment'></div>除已用应支外，所馀之数尚有若干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1208414_comment'></div>凡已往之费，不可追究，未来之费，所宜会也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1208414_comment'></div>前此朝廷遣使会计边费已用之数，所得者簿历盈车，不可覆考，重有烦费，无补于事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1208414_comment'></div>今臣所论者右曹根本之财而已，不知五敕所起可以为西边几年之用否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1208414_comment'></div>困天下之力，坏神考之政，而数年之后未免阙绝，庙堂之上今亦可以觉悟矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1208414_comment'></div>惟陛下熟计之，幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_101_1208414_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年8月25日</a>　瓘又录《上曾布书》、《日录辨》及《国用须知》具状三省。作品：申三省乞早行窜黜状。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷2784。）</span>与曾布书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》卷2784。）</span><div id='poem_1208446' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208446' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208446?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申三省乞早行窜黜状<span class='inlineComment2'>（建中靖国元年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年8月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208446")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208446_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208446'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208446'>昨诣尚书省投书，蒙中书相公面谕其详，谓瓘所论为元祐浅见单闻之说，兼言天下未尝乏才，虽有十书，布亦不动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208446_comment'></div>瓘不达大体，触忤大臣，除具申御史台乞赐弹劾外，伏乞敷奏，早行窜黜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1208446_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1208447' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208447' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208447?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与曾布书<span class='inlineComment2'>（建中靖国元年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年8月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208447")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208447_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208447'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208447'>瓘闻之，古贤未尝无过，周公、孔子、颜渊皆有过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208447_comment'></div>子路闻过则喜，所以为圣贤之徒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208447_comment'></div>成汤改过不吝，所以为百世之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208447_comment'></div>故曰：「过而能改，善莫大焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208447_comment'></div>匹夫改过，善在一身；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208447_comment'></div>大臣改过，福及天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208447_comment'></div>阁下德隆功大，四海之内所赞颂，然谓阁下无过则不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208447_comment'></div>尊私史而厌宗庙，缘边费而坏先政，此二者阁下之过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208447_comment'></div>违神考之志，坏神考之事，在此二者，天下所共知，而圣主不得闻其说，蒙蔽之患，孰大于此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208447_comment'></div>瓘之所撰《日录辨》一篇，已进之于上，阁下试一读之，则所谓尊私史而厌宗庙者可见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208447_comment'></div>瓘去年所论陕西、河东事，未尽详悉，近守无为，奉行朝廷诏敕，乃知天下根本之财，皆已运于西边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208447_comment'></div>比缘都司职事，看详内降劄子，因述其事，名曰《国用须知》，亦已进之于上，阁下试读之，则所谓缘边费而坏先政者可见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208447_comment'></div>主上修继述之效，阁下乃违志坏事，以为继述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208447_comment'></div>自今日已往，其效渐见，所以误吾君者，不亦大乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208447_comment'></div>效之速者，尤在于边费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208447_comment'></div>熙宁条例司之所讲，元丰右曹之所守，举朝公卿，无如阁下最知其本末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208447_comment'></div>今阁下独擅政柄，首坏先烈，弥缝壅蔽，人未敢议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208447_comment'></div>它日主上因此两事，以继述之事问于阁下，阁下将何以为对？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208447_comment'></div>当此之时，阁下虽有腹心之助，恐亦不得高枕而卧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208447_comment'></div>且边事之费，外则帅臣，内则宰相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208447_comment'></div>帅臣知一方之事而已，虽竭府库之财而倾之，不可责也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208447_comment'></div>至于宰相之任，则异乎此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208447_comment'></div>岂可以知天下匮竭，而恬不恤匮竭，因坏先政，因务蔽蒙，阁下欲辞其过，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208447_comment'></div>瓘比缘禀事，闻阁下之言，指尚书省为道揆之地，瓘谓阁下此言失矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208447_comment'></div>三省长官，宜守法而已，若夫道揆，天子三公之事，岂太宰之所得预乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208447_comment'></div>两年日食之变，皆在正阳之月，此乃臣道大彊之应，亦阁下之所当畏也，宜守而揆，岂抑畏之谓乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208447_comment'></div>《周官》曰：「居宠思危」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208447_comment'></div>今天下旱蝗，方数千里，天变屡作，人心忧惧，边费坏败，国用耗竭，而阁下方且以为得道揆之体，可谓居宠而不思危矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208447_comment'></div>阁下于瓘有荐进之恩，瓘不敢负，是以论吉凶之理，献先甲之言，冀有补于阁下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208447_comment'></div>若阁下不察其心，拒而不受，则今日之言，谓之负恩可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208447_comment'></div>负与不负在瓘，察与不察在阁下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1208447_comment'></div>事君之位无高下，各行其志，孰得而夺之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1208447_comment'></div>瓘去年九月三日上封章，皆乞奏知东朝，所以尊人主而抑外家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1208447_comment'></div>钦圣未见察，则瓘被贬黜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1208447_comment'></div>后来慈意开悟，则瓘得牵复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1208447_comment'></div>人主察孤臣之尽忠，钦圣知忠言之有补，母慈子孝，主圣臣直，此国家两全之道，庙社无疆之福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1208447_comment'></div>今钦圣纳忠之美未白于天下，而谏官不二之心得罪于庙堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1208447_comment'></div>胁持之风，甚于去岁，乖离之论，唱自大臣，所以厚钦慈者，果在此乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1208447_comment'></div>瓘前日辞都司之命，而阁下未许其去者，阁下必有以处瓘矣，此士大夫之所共谕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1208447_comment'></div>主上念钦圣纳忠之意，察孤臣不二之心，奖眷之恩，至深至厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1208447_comment'></div>瓘欲择死，所以图报效，无负于人主，无愧于外家，一身之安危，岂暇恤哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1208447_comment'></div>然则今日之言，安知不见察于阁下也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1208447_comment'></div>阁下深思而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1208447_comment'></div>瓘不敢供要职，重取烦言，又不忍嘿嘿而去，惟阁下留听，幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1208447_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年8月26日</a>　上令责瓘，乃以瓘知泰州。中书舍人邹浩、右谏议大夫陈次升均言不妥。<br /></div>
-----end
