-----title
宁波（鄞县）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b278256b70144c898ebd26a2e36a4291_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b278256b70144c898ebd26a2e36a4291");'><span id='b278256b70144c898ebd26a2e36a4291_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1094')">1091-1094年</a>，35-38岁</div><div id='b278256b70144c898ebd26a2e36a4291' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年</a>　通判明州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年11月27日</a>　十一月辛亥，作《顺昌济川桥记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年</a>　元祐之末，与王涣之、龚夬、张庭坚游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年</a>　通判明州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年</a>　通判明州，题咏甚多。作品：和刘太守洲诗。次韵袁朝请陪太守游湖心亭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（元祐八年守明州，疏月湖积土为十洲，随景命名，与舒亶唱和。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年7月11日</a>　通判明州，七月丙戌，作序。作品：《净土十疑论》后序。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年</a>　通判明州，应明州天童山景德寺住持可斋之请托，作记。作品：景德寺转轮藏记。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年4月20日</a>　通判明州，跋朱表臣所藏《欧阳六一居士贴》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　通判明州，章惇入相，道过山阳，瓘从众谒。惇闻其名，独邀与同载。劝惇以“清朋党，持中道”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　通判明州，跋朱表臣所藏《欧阳六一居士贴》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　通判明州，复除太学博士。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='9cbade367f2e4298a3dc32b0079ad126_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9cbade367f2e4298a3dc32b0079ad126");'><span id='9cbade367f2e4298a3dc32b0079ad126_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1110')">1106-1110年</a>，50-54岁</div><div id='9cbade367f2e4298a3dc32b0079ad126' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年</a>　移居明州，作诗。作品：和陶渊明归去来辞。<div id='poem_1208373' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208373' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208373?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和渊明归去来辞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1106年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208373")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208373_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208373'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208373'>归去来兮，人生之乐无如归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208373_comment'></div>舍躯命而不保，兹明哲之所悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208373_comment'></div>悼前言于既往，舌驷马兮焉追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208373_comment'></div>持孤愿以取戮，丛一身之百非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208373_comment'></div>心耿耿兮如醉，泪浪浪兮沾衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208373_comment'></div>情犬马兮恩厚，命蝼蚁兮力微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208373_comment'></div>乃瞻帝阙，梦驰心奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208373_comment'></div>俯步驽蹇，曾嘶君门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208373_comment'></div>筋力已竭，皮骨空存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208373_comment'></div>烟不染突，酒离空尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208373_comment'></div>纵伤戚之盈抱，遣饥渴而违颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208373_comment'></div>先众馁而独饱，非素怀之所安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208373_comment'></div>偶只影而南骛，度桂岭之遥关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208373_comment'></div>赖皇明之独照，迈曦娥而监观<span class='inlineComment2'>（逸句二。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208373_comment'></div>稽白刃于槁颈，察忠精之枅枅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208373_comment'></div>归去来兮，息心猿之外游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208373_comment'></div>觅波镜而不得，奚泡像之可求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208373_comment'></div>听自他之可幻，寂闲忙之两忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208373_comment'></div>吾既知之矣，又将以告乎朋俦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208373_comment'></div>事海无际，身如轻舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208373_comment'></div>葵转动以倾日，狐终尽而首丘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208373_comment'></div>金百死而不化，水万折而东流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208373_comment'></div>审物性之莫夺，戒馀习之未休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208373_comment'></div>已矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208373_comment'></div>岫云舒卷各有时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208373_comment'></div>出者自出，留者自留，谁能比迹而同之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208373_comment'></div>华胥非一途，游寝不可期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208373_comment'></div>谅饥穰之莫易，聊致力于耘耔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208373_comment'></div>感子牟之昨梦，继《天保》而成诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208373_comment'></div>虽死生之事大矣，安之若命复何疑？</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1208373_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年</a>　在明州，有跋文。作品：跋蔡群谟帖。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年9月28日</a>　在明州，跋苏东坡诗曲。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年</a>　在明州，作《四明尊尧集》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>　在明州，与陈禾相好，遣其子正汇从学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年8月</a>　在明州。八月甲寅朔，作《南湖净土院记》作品：南湖净土院记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（明智法师，即明州南湖延庆堂上讲主，瓘即受其请托，作《净土院记》）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年8月</a>　在明州。八月甲寅朔，有与明智法师书。作品：与明智法师书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（明智法师，即明州南湖延庆堂上讲主，瓘即受其请托，作《净土院记》）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年2月8日</a>　在明州。有记。作品：湖州开元寺观音记。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年11月20日</a>　在明州。跋杨中立撰陈居士传。作品：跋陈居士传。<span class='inlineComment2'>（该跋文见《龟山集》卷二十七，文渊阁四库全书本。）</span><div id='poem_1208464' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208464' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208464?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋杨时陈居士传</a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年11月20日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208464")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208464_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208464'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208464'>中立先生所撰《陈居士传》，予兄孙渐得其本，自馀杭来四明，出以示予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208464_comment'></div>先生言行信于天下，所以深嗟而屡叹之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208464_comment'></div>虽晦于今，后当显白，异时尚论之士可不考欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208464_comment'></div>予与居士同乡，而以不得见之为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208464_comment'></div>为写此传，以畀其子孙，使刻而藏之，以成先生论述之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208464_comment'></div>大观二年十一月二十二日，沙县陈瓘书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1208464_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年</a>　在明州。有诗文。作品：苏文饶往昌国意颇惮之送以诗因勉之。文饶自京师还欲往昌国而风作不可渡乃为绝句戏之。文饶自昌国以诗见寄次韵。送周初平（五首）<div id='poem_163998' class='_poem'><div 合浦
-----detail

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年</a>　任廉州编管。作词赠邹浩，且有书信往来。作品：蝶恋花。<div id='poem_164073' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_164073' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/164073?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蝶恋花</a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_164073")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_164073_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_164073'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_164073'>有个胡儿模样别。<div id='poem_sentence_0_164073_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_164073'>满颔髭须，生得浑如漆。<div id='poem_sentence_1_164073_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_164073'>见说近来头也白。<div id='poem_sentence_2_164073_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_164073'>髭须那得长长黑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_164073_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_164073'>□□□□□□□。<div id='poem_sentence_4_164073_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_164073'>籋子镊来，须有千堆雪。<div id='poem_sentence_5_164073_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_164073'>莫向细君容易说。<div id='poem_sentence_6_164073_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_164073'>恐他嫌你将伊摘。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_164073_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年</a>　任廉州编管。作词赠广陵马推官。作品：减字木兰花。<span class='inlineComment2'>（未知广陵马推官何许人。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年</a>　任廉州编管。陈之颜卒，瓘为其作墓志。作品：陈之翰墓志。<div id='poem_1208479' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208479' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208479?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈之翰墓志</a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208479")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208479_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208479'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208479'>之翰少有志操，治经求其大旨，为文不蹈袭陈语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208479_comment'></div>三上礼部不中第，归求其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208479_comment'></div>事继母曰孝，兄曰悌，弟曰友，朋友曰信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208479_comment'></div>陈氏赀故厚，君平于处治，不为纤啬，赀日益耗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208479_comment'></div>乡人初贷黄金，后携以偿，君适在汴舟，其人绐曰金误坠水，君不疑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208479_comment'></div>后数年，其人自悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208479_comment'></div>疾且死，遣其子来谢，致所当偿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208479_comment'></div>君受而不拒，徐以所偿助其丧葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208479_comment'></div>崇宁二年，诏举遗逸，鄞之贤士夫闻而相语曰：「此可以得宪之矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208479_comment'></div>州及部使者用众论荐君于朝，天子官之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208479_comment'></div>君气和言温，与人交，久而益恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208479_comment'></div>口不道人之过，平居若无营于世者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208479_comment'></div>尚论古人自春秋以来千馀年事，是非得失，阔略细故，取其大者论之，郁而始通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208479_comment'></div>方流而遽涸，非命也欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208479_comment'></div>卒时年六十，葬翔凤隐学山。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1208479_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年3月5日</a>　任廉州编管。作记。作品：了斋记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（瓘移廉州，在州宣化坊读书，名其斋曰“了斋”，著《合浦尊尧集》同必大《文忠集》卷47有《题陈忠肃公尊尧集稿》）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　任廉州编管。作《了斋易说》<div id='poem_163991' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_163991' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a -----title
南通（鄞县）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fd3f71058948459aa7e5cd7df4fcc35f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fd3f71058948459aa7e5cd7df4fcc35f");'><span id='fd3f71058948459aa7e5cd7df4fcc35f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1111')">1110-1111年</a>，54-55岁</div><div id='fd3f71058948459aa7e5cd7df4fcc35f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年3月</a>　诏瓘通州安置，上谢表。作品：通州安置谢表。<div id='poem_1208441' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208441' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208441?labeling=true' target='_blank'>通州安置谢表<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观四年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208441")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208441_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208441'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208441'>脱死幽缧，置身善地，上恩曲逮，孤涕横流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208441_comment'></div>伏念臣投窜之馀，年龄已暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208441_comment'></div>皆有自贻之戚，天实谴之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208441_comment'></div>灾非无妄而来，人谁矜者！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208441_comment'></div>议律难逃于常宪，原情独赖于清衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208441_comment'></div>积感弥深，论报无所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208441_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下则尧之大，用舜之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208441_comment'></div>宥罪每发于深慈，施刑宁失于过厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208441_comment'></div>不遗疏远，咸与并包。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208441_comment'></div>臣敢不上体宽仁，静思愆咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208441_comment'></div>终于屏迹，益坚爱主之诚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208441_comment'></div>死而有知，尚图结草之报。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1208441_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年</a>　在通州，与吴表臣定交。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年11月</a>　在通州。十一月，放自便，上谢表。作品：通州自便谢表。<div id='poem_1208442' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208442' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208442?labeling=true' target='_blank'>通州自便谢表<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观四年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208442")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208442_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208442'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208442'>恩由独断，泽被孤忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208442_comment'></div>刑部之执守虽坚，天子之福威无壅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208442_comment'></div>乃公朝之盛事，岂<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1208442", 1208442, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>小己</span>之私荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208442_comment'></div>恭叙感悰，仰渎高听<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208442_comment'></div>伏念臣昨蒙善贷，赐以生还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208442_comment'></div>萍迹孤睽，久寄食于异县；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208442_comment'></div>荜门干蛊，常委事于长男。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208442_comment'></div>所营不足以藩身，其出每缘于糊口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208442_comment'></div>去庭闱者累月，闻道路之一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208442_comment'></div>耳受而辄行，亲危而不顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208442_comment'></div>缘帅司深疾其生事，故传者多指为病狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208442_comment'></div>万口嗷嗷，两路詾詾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208442_comment'></div>狐突教子，素存不贰之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208442_comment'></div>曾参杀人，宁免至三之惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208442_comment'></div>事既匿而难晓，时浸久而益疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208442_comment'></div>制所深严，就逮于重江之外；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208442_comment'></div>狱辞平允，阅实于片言之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208442_comment'></div>矜其无罪之可书，许以还家而自便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208442_comment'></div>出圜扉而涕感，瞻魏阙而神留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208442_comment'></div>寻沐宽恩，移置近地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208442_comment'></div>海岛万里，不如无子之无忧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208442_comment'></div>淮壖一身，弥觉有生之有患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208442_comment'></div>擢发不足以数臣之罪，沥血不足以写臣之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208442_comment'></div>羔羊之性自公，犬马之情爱主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208442_comment'></div>忘身徇国，初无系吝之私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208442_comment'></div>抱疾呼天，惟恃精诚之格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208442_comment'></div>忽因诏谕，特免拘维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208442_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下尧大并容，舜明洞照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208442_comment'></div>人人皆使之得所，事事唯恐其有偏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208442_comment'></div>继志用神考之心，应天以格王之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208442_comment'></div>旧弊若冰之将释，新庆如川之方流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1208442_comment'></div>家国平康，内外交泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1208442_comment'></div>遂使赦无留令，昔阻隔而今行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1208442_comment'></div>士有宿愆，始弃置而终宥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1208442_comment'></div>全家荷德，无路酬恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1208442_comment'></div>蝼蚁之力至微，但知恭顺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1208442_comment'></div>蒲柳之身已老，尚可糜捐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1208442_comment'></div>望天虽隔于戴盆，向日敢忘于倾藿<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1208442_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_1208442'>「中谢」二字原无，据《唐宋元名表》补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1208442_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1208442_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1208442'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_37_1208442_0'>⑴ 《皇朝文鉴》卷七一。又见《通鉴长编纪事本末》卷一二九，《陈了翁年谱》附录，《唐宋元名表》卷下之一。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1208442_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年1月</a>　在通州。正月，诏明州取陈瓘《尊尧集》送编修政典局，从张商英建请也。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年4月</a>　在通州。作墓志铭。作品：陈宪之墓志铭。<div id='poem_1208478' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208478' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208478?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐充之墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208478")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208478_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208478'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208478'>充之姓唐氏，讳广仁，充之字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208478_comment'></div>其先幽州人，自石晋割地，至五世祖始得从归沧州乐陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208478_comment'></div>咸平中，曾祖克勤被诏试武艺，授三班借职，以天雄军管界巡检使卒于官，因家焉，遂为大名内黄人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208478_comment'></div>祖中立，大名司法参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208478_comment'></div>父愈，喜儒士，自充之五六岁时训以诗书，浸长使从学于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208478_comment'></div>充之能择交游，言行谨饬，读经史，讲义理，亦长于科举之习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208478_comment'></div>中元祐六年进士第，调乾宁军司法参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208478_comment'></div>界河驿有杀略人者，守将械送狱，俾鞫之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208478_comment'></div>疑其诬服，以白守，守不信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208478_comment'></div>方趣决不已，而霸州获真盗，然后释无罪者凡四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208478_comment'></div>后为常州录事参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208478_comment'></div>部使者闻充之在乾宁有审克之誉，部有疑讼，多以属之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208478_comment'></div>充之所辨正合人情者非止一事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208478_comment'></div>改官制，授通仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208478_comment'></div>以荐者及格，当改官，坐元符末上书，命格不下，调监寿州开顺口盐矾酒税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208478_comment'></div>未赴，丁母忧，服阕，监苏州酒税务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208478_comment'></div>郡守李尚书孝寿治尚峻猛，不任僚属，充之权幕官，敢与论曲直，苏人多赖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208478_comment'></div>后守盛待制章于充之为姻家，初与充之善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208478_comment'></div>郡人朱氏有势焰，守所歆慕，众皆帖帖屈随，而充之一切自异，著憎慢之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208478_comment'></div>守不能堪，众或怒，置充之于狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208478_comment'></div>吹毛无实，以酤酒点饶为罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208478_comment'></div>充之既废，贫困不能北归，居楚之宝应，益以读书教子为事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208478_comment'></div>又七年，以疾卒于家，宣和己亥五月丙辰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208478_comment'></div>以某年某月某日甲子，葬于扬州之某地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208478_comment'></div>充之娶张氏，中散大夫某之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208478_comment'></div>子男四人，曰激、曰浚、曰渤、曰洪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208478_comment'></div>女四人，长适从事郎赵枋，馀未嫁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208478_comment'></div>初，充之客寓宝应，茍营屋室，而勉竭其力，以择葬地于维扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208478_comment'></div>躬诣内黄，启祖考之殡，迎护以来，将卜日历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208478_comment'></div>盖奔走自效，服勤累岁，未克<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1208478", 1208478, "Clauses/94/Comments/0")'>迁奉</span>，而充之得疾卒矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208478_comment'></div>今其子激等既葬充之，又能率先志，并襄大事，使三世窀穸之事讫无可憾，亦可以见充之身教之遗美矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1208478_comment'></div>激等遣人自宝应来南康，以吕本中所状充之之行求铭于瓘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1208478_comment'></div>书辞惨切，且曰：「先人疾亟时，尝问曰：『居仁约访我，尚未到』？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1208478_comment'></div>又叹曰：『我欲一游庐山，今不能矣』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1208478_comment'></div>诸孤不肖，摧割待尽，念欲毕闻馀训，永不可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1208478_comment'></div>维行状既获所属，而砻石穴土，以需于掩圹之后者，将孰请而可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1208478_comment'></div>居仁，本中字也，正献公之曾孙，言行有家法，其所叙次皆可考證。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1208478_comment'></div>其载充之教子之言曰：「涑水文正公尝谓平生无以过人，但事无大小皆可使人知尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1208478_comment'></div>汝曹不可一日忘此语也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1208478_comment'></div>濉阳刘公尝谓充之材用有馀，遽闻其死，嗟惜不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1208478_comment'></div>呜呼，可达可寿，而废斥夭短，岂非命欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1208478_comment'></div>其所厚善，率皆迟钝迂阔之士，于其殁也，能相与戚嗟而已，悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1208478_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_1208478'>木摇难栖，波涌莫济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1208478_comment'></div>穮蓘积劳，未穰而逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1208478_comment'></div>饥穰天也，人岂能违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1208478_comment'></div>奄忽不俟，岂唯我悲。</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1208478_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年5月</a>　在通州。再下通州取陈瓘《尊尧集》送编修政典局，瓘上表。作品：进四明尊尧集表。<div id='poem_1208443' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208443' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208443?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进四明尊尧集表</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和元年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208443")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208443_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208443'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208443'>臣某言：臣六月初五日准通州牒，准编修政典局牒奉圣旨，取臣所著《尊尧集》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208443_comment'></div>臣依禀圣旨，不敢<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1208443", 1208443, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>违滞</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208443_comment'></div>缘臣著撰此集，未经奏御，今具状申编修政典局，乞为缴进，合于御前开拆者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208443_comment'></div>臣窃以畎亩爱君，精诚虽至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208443_comment'></div>刍荛议政，迂阔难行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208443_comment'></div>葵向不习而常倾，芹陋敢期于得献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208443_comment'></div>独因睿断，许贡危衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208443_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣粪土下材，犬马贱质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208443_comment'></div>数罪固多于擢发，舍生无意于兼鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208443_comment'></div>初欲糜捐，终难缄默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208443_comment'></div>因续前言之绪，聊输垂绝之忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208443_comment'></div>非敢有善善恶恶之辞，但欲明尊尊卑卑之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208443_comment'></div>此蝼蚁所能知也，在搢绅安可藐然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208443_comment'></div>八十卷之私书，夺此与彼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208443_comment'></div>十九年之懿绩，可从而违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208443_comment'></div>陛下于继述之初，首辨明于兹事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208443_comment'></div>微臣持将顺之志，在流窜而靡忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208443_comment'></div>铺张痛诋之言，编类厚诬之语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208443_comment'></div>初谓熙宁之辅，不愧有商之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208443_comment'></div>于成汤敢肆厥欺，疑安石有所弗忍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208443_comment'></div>及究观于怼笔，始粗见其游辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208443_comment'></div>因思大典之久诬，益愿忘躯而往诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208443_comment'></div>合浦十论，申旧疏之馀言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208443_comment'></div>四明八门，撮其要于一序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208443_comment'></div>实欲彰火德之盛，不敢畏王氏之强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208443_comment'></div>宁碎首于邦诛，忍谩心于国是？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208443_comment'></div>彼效尤于往辙，亦茍逞于陈编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208443_comment'></div>难以缕窥，略举纲要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208443_comment'></div>谓艺祖滥诛无罪，谓真宗矫诬上天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208443_comment'></div>讪薄裕陵，攘夺先美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208443_comment'></div>以托训为钳口之术，以归过为自誉之媒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1208443_comment'></div>但矜诋訾之极工，罔顾威灵之如在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1208443_comment'></div>几乎骂矣，岂不痛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1208443_comment'></div>读其书宁忍终篇，稽其文可为流涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1208443_comment'></div>代言之笔，尽目其徒为儒宗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1208443_comment'></div>首善之宫，肇塑其形为坐像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1208443_comment'></div>礼官舞礼而行谄，史书献佞而请观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1208443_comment'></div>光乎仲尼，乃子雱圣父之赞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1208443_comment'></div>比诸孔子，实卞等轻君之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1208443_comment'></div>彼衰周之僻王，弃真儒之将圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1208443_comment'></div>当时不得配太庙之飨，后世所以广上丁之祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1208443_comment'></div>今比安石为钦王之臣，则方神考为何代之主？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1208443_comment'></div>又况一人幸学，列辟班随，至尊拜伏于炉前，故臣骄倨而坐视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1208443_comment'></div>百官气郁，多士心寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1208443_comment'></div>自有华夏以来，无此悖倒之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1208443_comment'></div>神考之再相安石，始终不过乎九年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1208443_comment'></div>安石之屏迹金陵，弃置不召者十载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1208443_comment'></div>八字威加于邓绾，万机独运于元丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1208443_comment'></div>岂可于善述之时，忽崇此不逊之像？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1208443_comment'></div>因坏先朝三舍之法，遂费今日千倍之财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1208443_comment'></div>人材之可擢不殊，国用之添费徒广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1208443_comment'></div>脧吾民之膏血，增彼像之精神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1208443_comment'></div>美成其私，怨集于国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1208443_comment'></div>陆贽设枝颠之喻，承业以财尽为忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1208443_comment'></div>忠哉古人爱君之诚，异乎今日养士之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1208443_comment'></div>又况临川之所学，不以《春秋》为可行，谓天子有北面之仪，谓君臣有迭宾之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1208443_comment'></div>礼仪如彼，名分若何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1208443_comment'></div>此乃衰世侮君之非，岂是先王访道之法？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1208443_comment'></div>赣川旧学，记刊于四纪之前；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1208443_comment'></div>辟水新廱，像成于一婿之手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1208443_comment'></div>唱如声召，应若响随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1208443_comment'></div>使王氏寖至于强梁，乃元祐助发其气燄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1208443_comment'></div>昔宣仁权同之际，谓介甫节行甚高，宜赠崇官，仍加美谥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1208443_comment'></div>司马光书之于简，吕公著行之于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1208443_comment'></div>不以稽弊为心，徒发镇浮之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1208443_comment'></div>负安石者重加黜责，欺神考者略不谁何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1208443_comment'></div>遂至于枝蔓而难图，岂非由偏助之太过？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1208443_comment'></div>虽当时未见诬史，而先朝自有圣批。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1208443_comment'></div>恬不奉行，养成乖悖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1208443_comment'></div>蒙蔽裕陵之众美，眩耀钟山之一书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1208443_comment'></div>四辅之行谋画，本生于《日录》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1208443_comment'></div>三卫之设规模，初定于新经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1208443_comment'></div>密密乎邓、蹇之安排，草草乎京、摅之传授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1208443_comment'></div>考其音声，则篪唱而埙和；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1208443_comment'></div>譬诸手足，则左弱而右强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1208443_comment'></div>凝为冰山，烈若原火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1208443_comment'></div>愚公老矣，益坚平险之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1208443_comment'></div>精卫眇然，未舍填波之愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1208443_comment'></div>殁而后已，志不可渝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1208443_comment'></div>望虽隔于戴盆，梦不忘于驰阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1208443_comment'></div>丹诚上格，天语遥询。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1208443_comment'></div>要观尊主之恭，缓议奸时之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1208443_comment'></div>渊冰在念，枭磔宁逃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1208443_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下天大普容，日明遍照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1208443_comment'></div>览熙丰记动之史，仿虞夏采诗之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1208443_comment'></div>咨舆议于多方，證私书之百毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1208443_comment'></div>舜纂尧绪，孜孜乎善继之勤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1208443_comment'></div>武广文声，斤斤乎丕承之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1208443_comment'></div>兹所谓一人之庆，可以得万国之欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1208443_comment'></div>凡有识知，孰不将顺？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1208443_comment'></div>天地尊卑之已定，首足上下之宜分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1208443_comment'></div>孔志在乎《春秋》，汉律严于名分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1208443_comment'></div>戴上者皆知此义，尊尧者岂独臣书？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1208443_comment'></div>燕马以市骨为先，鬻骥者必将来矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1208443_comment'></div>郑校决防川之壅，有舌者其忍默乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1208443_comment'></div>臣命可危，众口难遏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1208443_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下念臣役志于享上，悯臣积祸于敢恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1208443_comment'></div>以尺朽之废材，贡一得之愚虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1208443_comment'></div>言多妄发，事则有稽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1208443_comment'></div>宣宗当绍宪之时，宁容德裕之夺语；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1208443_comment'></div>武帝以述景为事，忍视马迁之短辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1208443_comment'></div>父子至情，古今一揆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1208443_comment'></div>不徵谤史之罪，则何以谢过于宗庙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1208443_comment'></div>不毁坐像之悖，则何以示顺于华夷？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1208443_comment'></div>国是方强，势难遽改；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1208443_comment'></div>大器至重，要在深思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1208443_comment'></div>庶乎苗莠之分，始于冠屦之辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1208443_comment'></div>至美成于刚健，大患生乎因循。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1208443_comment'></div>儒宗数人，自是一家之说；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1208443_comment'></div>圣主独断，乃为我宋之休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1208443_comment'></div>天心笃爱之甚明，人情企想而有待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1208443_comment'></div>解神考在天之怒，成圣主奉先之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1208443_comment'></div>克果断于蔡方，人将大觉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1208443_comment'></div>善光扬于尧绩，上可无为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1208443_comment'></div>于一颦一笑之中，成允文允武之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1208443_comment'></div>臣将献骏惠太平之颂，岂特进狂简不裁之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1208443_comment'></div>胸臆无奇，但尽恭于文字；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1208443_comment'></div>筋骸已惫，当致命于君亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1208443_comment'></div>仰酬再造之恩，退听一成之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1208443_comment'></div>阖门待尽，殒首知归<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1208443_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_120_1208443'>「中谢」二字原无，据《播芳大全》补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_120_1208443_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1208443'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_119_1208443_0'>⑴ 《皇朝文鉴》卷七一。又见《四明尊尧集》卷首，《五百家播芳大全文粹》卷二下，《桯史》卷一一，《唐宋元名表》卷下之一。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1208443_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年7月</a>　在通州。有跋文。作品：跋司马温公简后。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年9月21日</a>　在通州。诏瓘特勒停，送台州羁管。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='86a7d4147c79492e8ce67803347dbd2f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("86a7d4147c79492e8ce67803347dbd2f");'><span id='86a7d4147c79492e8ce67803347dbd2f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年</a>，59岁</div><div id='86a7d4147c79492e8ce67803347dbd2f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年3月17日</a>　瓘以承事郎叙官自便，自台州归通州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年8月</a>　与李纲定交于姑苏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年3月28日</a>　在通州，有跋。作品：跋黄尚书送左经臣序。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
临海
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f0cf6f6edad54c6888646cb1329f5ab9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f0cf6f6edad54c6888646cb1329f5ab9");'><span id='f0cf6f6edad54c6888646cb1329f5ab9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1115')">1111-1115年</a>，55-59岁</div><div id='f0cf6f6edad54c6888646cb1329f5ab9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年11月10日</a>　十一月已巳到时台州，上表。作品：台州羁管谢表。<div id='poem_1208444' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208444' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208444?labeling=true' target='_blank'>台州羁管谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和元年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208444")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208444_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208444'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208444'>臣瓘言：政和元年六月初五日，准通州牒，准编修政典局牒，奉旨取索臣所撰《尊尧集》，请速为检取，封角交付差去人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208444_comment'></div>续又准通州牒，《尊尧集》系奉圣旨取索，不可迟缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208444_comment'></div>臣即于六月十九日申通州迄，依圣旨发递前去，仍申编修政典局云：「上件《尊尧集》先合奏御，今匣内黄帕文字等并题作臣瓘谨封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208444_comment'></div>伏望本局特为进入，于御前开拆」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208444_comment'></div>今于十月初七日，准通州牒，准尚书刑部符，都省劄子：「奉圣旨：陈瓘自撰《尊尧集》，语言无绪，尽系诋诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208444_comment'></div>不行毁弃，送与张商英，意要行用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208444_comment'></div>特勒停，送台州羁管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208444_comment'></div>令本州当职官常切觉察，不得放出州城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208444_comment'></div>月具存在，申尚书省」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208444_comment'></div>臣即时望阙谢恩，发离本家，水陆兼行，不敢住滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208444_comment'></div>今于十一月初十日巳时到台州城内者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208444_comment'></div>畎亩之志，一书可通；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208444_comment'></div>刍荛之言，万里不隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208444_comment'></div>集群词而上达，遭一览以为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208444_comment'></div>窜路虽遥，陈情已毕<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208444_comment'></div>伏念臣材如粪土，身若梗蓬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208444_comment'></div>非敢以著书为能，所陈者戴君之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208444_comment'></div>知诋诬之不可，志在尊尧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208444_comment'></div>岂行用之敢私，心唯助舜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208444_comment'></div>语言无绪，议论至迂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208444_comment'></div>独归美于先猷，遂大违于国是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208444_comment'></div>不行毁弃，有误咨询。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208444_comment'></div>虚消十载之光阴，靡恤一门之沟壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208444_comment'></div>果烦揆路，特建刑章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208444_comment'></div>若非恃庇于九重，安能延龄于再造？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208444_comment'></div>由淮入浙，自通至台，怒涛虽阻于重江，毒瘴幸殊于五岭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208444_comment'></div>尚留顶踵，独赖君亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208444_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下天大并容，日明洞照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208444_comment'></div>以至慈而善贷，推观过之深仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208444_comment'></div>悯此颠隮，欲其存在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208444_comment'></div>以身藏怨，蝼蚁之命至微；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1208444_comment'></div>徇国捐生，犬马之心未替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1208444_comment'></div>梦驰丹阙，日想清光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1208444_comment'></div>重干擢发之诛，徒郁戴盆之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1208444_comment'></div>馀生易舍，大德难酬。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1208444_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年</a>　在台州，有文。作品：谏后疏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　羁管台州，与徐中行定交。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年2月2日</a>　羁管台州，有文。作品：跋张氏边事札子。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年8月9日</a>　羁管台州，作文。作品：责沈。<div id='poem_1208458' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208458' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208458?labeling=true' target='_blank'>责沈文贻知默侄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208458")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208458_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208458'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208458'>适越而北辕，越不可至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208458_comment'></div>徙越人而置于齐里，则越语可易而为齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208458_comment'></div>然则气质一定，而不能自易其习者，非以其不学欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208458_comment'></div>气质之用狭，道学之力大，习其所自习者未尝察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208458_comment'></div>天气而地质，无物不然，人藐乎其间，亦一物耳，物与物奚以相远？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208458_comment'></div>或哲或愚，不系其习乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208458_comment'></div>思诚之道，莫先于学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208458_comment'></div>务学之要，在于求师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208458_comment'></div>颜子之不迁不贰得于孔子，希颜之人将孰师焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208458_comment'></div>叶公问孔子于子路，子路不对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208458_comment'></div>夫叶公有知人之明，有谋国之忠，爱贤而得民，慎微而忧远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208458_comment'></div>其事皆有可指，其遗语之记于《缁衣》者亦可观焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208458_comment'></div>楚国之贤，谁出其右？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208458_comment'></div>子路非慢贤者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208458_comment'></div>鲁有仲尼，而彼不知焉，则于其问也，何足对哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208458_comment'></div>陈良楚产也，而能使北方之学者莫或先之，故孟子以良为豪杰之士，为其能悦周公、孔子之道而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208458_comment'></div>不知仲尼，则虽贤如子高，亦孔门之所不对也，为士而稽古者可不鉴哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208458_comment'></div>予元丰乙丑夏为礼部贡院点检官，适与校书郎范公醇夫同舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208458_comment'></div>公尝论颜子之不迁不贰，惟伯淳有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208458_comment'></div>予问公曰：「伯淳谁也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208458_comment'></div>公默然久之，曰：「不知有程伯淳耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208458_comment'></div>予谢曰：「生长东南，实未知也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208458_comment'></div>时予年二十有九矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208458_comment'></div>自是以来，常以寡陋自愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208458_comment'></div>得其传者，如杨中立先生，亦未之识也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208458_comment'></div>崇宁之初，兄孙渐就学其门，时予在合浦，始获通问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208458_comment'></div>予之内讼改过，赖其一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208458_comment'></div>渐于是时，亦以所闻警予之缪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208458_comment'></div>予始忽其言，久而后知其为药石也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208458_comment'></div>今渐来天台，考其学益进，闻其言益可喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208458_comment'></div>陶染薰铸，有自来矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1208458_comment'></div>举修步于南溟，观洪澜于北壑，此可远之基也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1208458_comment'></div>始之不谋，何以得此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1208458_comment'></div>古之善学者，心远而莫御，然后气融而无间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1208458_comment'></div>物格而不二，然后养熟而道凝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1208458_comment'></div>山上有木，其进也渐，合抱之干，岂一朝一夕之所可俟哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1208458_comment'></div>人之患在不立其基，基立而不勉，亦何以愈于彼乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1208458_comment'></div>物之终始，可不严哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1208458_comment'></div>始识而终成，同乎一默，非言语所能究也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1208458_comment'></div>予以多言取祸，尚未诛殛，戴恩自幸，不知岁月之久，而生死之有二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1208458_comment'></div>既老且病，手痹目昏，简编笔砚，殆将捐弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1208458_comment'></div>今于渐之行，不能忘言，作《责沈》以贻之，喜渐之能谋其始，而笃之使有成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1208458_comment'></div>政和三年八月九日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1208458_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　羁管台州，有诗。作品：送几叟诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年</a>　羁管台州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年10月19日</a>　羁管台州，有跋文。作品：跋江左司劝菩提心文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年</a>　羁管台州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年</a>　羁管台州，有跋文。作品：跋张承老所藏纱元忠司谏简。书孙元忠上刘萃老甘赋后。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年</a>　羁管台州，曾作诗。作品：答瑞岩湛老。和邓鲠之韵。<div id='poem_164024' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_164024' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/164024?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答瑞岩湛老</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_164024")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_164024_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_164024'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_164024'>示我超然句，能令滞念开。<div id='poem_sentence_0_164024_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_164024'>盍移瑞岩刹，为我入城来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_164024_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_164024'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_164024_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_164033' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_164033' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/164033?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和邓鲠之韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_164033")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_164033_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_164033'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_164033'>十年三谪海边州，洛口相望阻献酬。<div id='poem_sentence_0_164033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_164033'>曾寄远诗来合浦，又传新句落丹丘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_164033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_164033'>身如古柏童童老，心似平江湛湛流。<div id='poem_sentence_2_164033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_164033'>归鸟倦飞云入岫，一瓢堪乐莫回头<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_164033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_164033'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_164033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_164033'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_164033_0'>⑴ 以上宋林表民《天台续集别编》卷二</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_164033_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年10月</a>　羁管台州，十月朔，陈瑊卒，瓘为其作墓志铭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年</a>　羁管台州，作文。作品：有门颂。直观坐禅法要记。跋黄裳委羽居士集序。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
九江（德化）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='26bdb583b23d45a4a5fb815f2a754d1d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("26bdb583b23d45a4a5fb815f2a754d1d");'><span id='26bdb583b23d45a4a5fb815f2a754d1d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年</a>，60岁</div><div id='26bdb583b23d45a4a5fb815f2a754d1d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年1月</a>　闰正月，瓘移江州居住，管勾江州太平观。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年8月15日</a>　在江州任，有祭文。作品：祭邓南夫文。<br /></div>

-----title
星子
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='449f745f3db241509980943f6f6a7bea_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("449f745f3db241509980943f6f6a7bea");'><span id='449f745f3db241509980943f6f6a7bea_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1119')">1117-1119年</a>，61-63岁</div><div id='449f745f3db241509980943f6f6a7bea' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年12月</a>　自江州移南康军居住。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年</a>　居南康军，作墓志铭。作品：中奉大夫游公墓志铭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1118')">1118年</a>　居南康军。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1118')">1118年</a>　居南康军，有诗。作品：送侄刚胜柔诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年5月</a>　居南康军。唐广仁卒，作墓铭。作品：唐充之墓志铭。<div id='poem_1208478' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208478' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208478?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐充之墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208478")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208478_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208478'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208478'>充之姓唐氏，讳广仁，充之字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208478_comment'></div>其先幽州人，自石晋割地，至五世祖始得从归沧州乐陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208478_comment'></div>咸平中，曾祖克勤被诏试武艺，授三班借职，以天雄军管界巡检使卒于官，因家焉，遂为大名内黄人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208478_comment'></div>祖中立，大名司法参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208478_comment'></div>父愈，喜儒士，自充之五六岁时训以诗书，浸长使从学于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208478_comment'></div>充之能择交游，言行谨饬，读经史，讲义理，亦长于科举之习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208478_comment'></div>中元祐六年进士第，调乾宁军司法参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208478_comment'></div>界河驿有杀略人者，守将械送狱，俾鞫之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208478_comment'></div>疑其诬服，以白守，守不信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208478_comment'></div>方趣决不已，而霸州获真盗，然后释无罪者凡四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208478_comment'></div>后为常州录事参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208478_comment'></div>部使者闻充之在乾宁有审克之誉，部有疑讼，多以属之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208478_comment'></div>充之所辨正合人情者非止一事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208478_comment'></div>改官制，授通仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208478_comment'></div>以荐者及格，当改官，坐元符末上书，命格不下，调监寿州开顺口盐矾酒税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208478_comment'></div>未赴，丁母忧，服阕，监苏州酒税务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208478_comment'></div>郡守李尚书孝寿治尚峻猛，不任僚属，充之权幕官，敢与论曲直，苏人多赖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208478_comment'></div>后守盛待制章于充之为姻家，初与充之善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208478_comment'></div>郡人朱氏有势焰，守所歆慕，众皆帖帖屈随，而充之一切自异，著憎慢之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208478_comment'></div>守不能堪，众或怒，置充之于狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208478_comment'></div>吹毛无实，以酤酒点饶为罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208478_comment'></div>充之既废，贫困不能北归，居楚之宝应，益以读书教子为事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208478_comment'></div>又七年，以疾卒于家，宣和己亥五月丙辰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208478_comment'></div>以某年某月某日甲子，葬于扬州之某地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208478_comment'></div>充之娶张氏，中散大夫某之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208478_comment'></div>子男四人，曰激、曰浚、曰渤、曰洪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208478_comment'></div>女四人，长适从事郎赵枋，馀未嫁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208478_comment'></div>初，充之客寓宝应，茍营屋室，而勉竭其力，以择葬地于维扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208478_comment'></div>躬诣内黄，启祖考之殡，迎护以来，将卜日历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208478_comment'></div>盖奔走自效，服勤累岁，未克<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1208478", 1208478, "Clauses/94/Comments/0")'>迁奉</span>，而充之得疾卒矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208478_comment'></div>今其子激等既葬充之，又能率先志，并襄大事，使三世窀穸之事讫无可憾，亦可以见充之身教之遗美矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1208478_comment'></div>激等遣人自宝应来南康，以吕本中所状充之之行求铭于瓘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1208478_comment'></div>书辞惨切，且曰：「先人疾亟时，尝问曰：『居仁约访我，尚未到』？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1208478_comment'></div>又叹曰：『我欲一游庐山，今不能矣』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1208478_comment'></div>诸孤不肖，摧割待尽，念欲毕闻馀训，永不可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1208478_comment'></div>维行状既获所属，而砻石穴土，以需于掩圹之后者，将孰请而可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1208478_comment'></div>居仁，本中字也，正献公之曾孙，言行有家法，其所叙次皆可考證。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1208478_comment'></div>其载充之教子之言曰：「涑水文正公尝谓平生无以过人，但事无大小皆可使人知尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1208478_comment'></div>汝曹不可一日忘此语也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1208478_comment'></div>濉阳刘公尝谓充之材用有馀，遽闻其死，嗟惜不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1208478_comment'></div>呜呼，可达可寿，而废斥夭短，岂非命欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1208478_comment'></div>其所厚善，率皆迟钝迂阔之士，于其殁也，能相与戚嗟而已，悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1208478_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_1208478'>木摇难栖，波涌莫济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1208478_comment'></div>穮蓘积劳，未穰而逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1208478_comment'></div>饥穰天也，人岂能违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1208478_comment'></div>奄忽不俟，岂唯我悲。</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1208478_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>　居南康军。有《答李纲书》，以翟梁公、李文靖、王文正之事业相勉。<div id='poem_1208448' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208448' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208448?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答杨中立游定夫书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208448")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208448_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208448'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208448'>康节云：「先天图，心法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208448_comment'></div>图虽无文，吾终日言，未尝离乎是」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208448_comment'></div>故其诗曰：「身在天地后，心在天地先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208448_comment'></div>天地自我出，自馀恶足言」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208448_comment'></div>又云：「数往者顺，知来者逆」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208448_comment'></div>此一节直解图意，如逆知四时之比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208448_comment'></div>然则先天之学，以心为本，其在经世者，康节之馀事耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208448_comment'></div>世学求《易》于文字，至语《皇极》，则或以为考数之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208448_comment'></div>康节诗云：「自从三度绝韦编，不读书来十二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208448_comment'></div>俯仰之间无所愧，任人谤道是神仙」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208448_comment'></div>同时者目其人为神仙，后来者名其书为考数，皆康节之所不憾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208448_comment'></div>乃其心，则务三圣而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208448_comment'></div>《观物》云：「起《震》终《艮》一节，明文王之八卦也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208448_comment'></div>天地定位一节，明伏羲之八卦也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208448_comment'></div>盖先天之学，本乎伏羲，而备于文王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208448_comment'></div>故其诗曰：「天地定位，《否》《泰》反类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208448_comment'></div>山泽通气，《咸》《损》见义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208448_comment'></div>雷风相薄，《恒》《益》起意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208448_comment'></div>水火相射，《既济》《未济》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208448_comment'></div>四象相交，成十六事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208448_comment'></div>八卦相荡，为六十四」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208448_comment'></div>八卦者，《易》之小成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208448_comment'></div>六十四卦者，《易》之大成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208448_comment'></div>集伏羲、文王之事而成之者，非孔子而谁乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208448_comment'></div>康节尝谓：「孟子未尝及《易》一字，而《易》道存焉，但人见之者鲜」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208448_comment'></div>又曰：「人能用《易》，是为知《易」》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208448_comment'></div>若孟子可谓善用《易》者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208448_comment'></div>夫《易》，「穷则变，变则通，通则久」，故圣人之用《易》，阖辟于未然，变其穷而通之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208448_comment'></div>若夫暑之穷也，变而为寒，寒之穷也，变而为暑，则是自变而自通者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208448_comment'></div>自变自通，复何赖于圣人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208448_comment'></div>子云赞《易》而非与《易》竞，孟子用《易》而语不及焉，此所谓贤者识其大者，其去圣人之用也，不为远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1208448_comment'></div>然而，或非《太玄》为覆瓿之书，或跻孟子于既圣之列，私论害公，意有所在，阖此于未然，岂乏人哉，奈何其无益也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1208448_comment'></div>《观物》云：「防乎其防，邦家其长，子孙其昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1208448_comment'></div>是以圣人重未然之防，是谓《易》之大纲」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1208448_comment'></div>而其诵孔子所以尽三才之道者，则曰：「行无辙迹，至妙至妙，在一动一静之间而已矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1208448_comment'></div>阐先圣之幽，微先天之显，不在康节之书乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1208448_comment'></div>虽在康节之书，而书亦不足以尽其奥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1208448_comment'></div>故司马文正与康节同时友善，而未尝有一言及先天学，其著《家范》，本于《家人》一卦，而尽取王弼之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1208448_comment'></div>今之说《易》者，方且厌常出奇，离日用而凿太空也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1208448_comment'></div>又或谓文正公疑先天之学，此岂足以语二公弛张之意乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1208448_comment'></div>二公不可得而见矣，瓘徒见其书，而欲窥其心，然乎否耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1208448_comment'></div>当先觉之任者，愿赐一言，庶几终可以无大过也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1208448_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>　居南康军。又跋张元干大父手泽。作品：跋张元干大父手泽。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》称《跋张元干幽岩尊祖事实》）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>　居南康军。曾作陈子真墓志铭。<div id='poem_1208478' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1208478' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1208478?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐充之墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34462, "北宋", "陈瓘", "poem_title_1208478")'>陈瓘</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1208478_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1208478'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1208478'>充之姓唐氏，讳广仁，充之字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1208478_comment'></div>其先幽州人，自石晋割地，至五世祖始得从归沧州乐陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1208478_comment'></div>咸平中，曾祖克勤被诏试武艺，授三班借职，以天雄军管界巡检使卒于官，因家焉，遂为大名内黄人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1208478_comment'></div>祖中立，大名司法参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1208478_comment'></div>父愈，喜儒士，自充之五六岁时训以诗书，浸长使从学于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1208478_comment'></div>充之能择交游，言行谨饬，读经史，讲义理，亦长于科举之习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1208478_comment'></div>中元祐六年进士第，调乾宁军司法参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1208478_comment'></div>界河驿有杀略人者，守将械送狱，俾鞫之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1208478_comment'></div>疑其诬服，以白守，守不信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1208478_comment'></div>方趣决不已，而霸州获真盗，然后释无罪者凡四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1208478_comment'></div>后为常州录事参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1208478_comment'></div>部使者闻充之在乾宁有审克之誉，部有疑讼，多以属之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1208478_comment'></div>充之所辨正合人情者非止一事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1208478_comment'></div>改官制，授通仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1208478_comment'></div>以荐者及格，当改官，坐元符末上书，命格不下，调监寿州开顺口盐矾酒税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1208478_comment'></div>未赴，丁母忧，服阕，监苏州酒税务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1208478_comment'></div>郡守李尚书孝寿治尚峻猛，不任僚属，充之权幕官，敢与论曲直，苏人多赖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1208478_comment'></div>后守盛待制章于充之为姻家，初与充之善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1208478_comment'></div>郡人朱氏有势焰，守所歆慕，众皆帖帖屈随，而充之一切自异，著憎慢之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1208478_comment'></div>守不能堪，众或怒，置充之于狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1208478_comment'></div>吹毛无实，以酤酒点饶为罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1208478_comment'></div>充之既废，贫困不能北归，居楚之宝应，益以读书教子为事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1208478_comment'></div>又七年，以疾卒于家，宣和己亥五月丙辰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1208478_comment'></div>以某年某月某日甲子，葬于扬州之某地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1208478_comment'></div>充之娶张氏，中散大夫某之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1208478_comment'></div>子男四人，曰激、曰浚、曰渤、曰洪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1208478_comment'></div>女四人，长适从事郎赵枋，馀未嫁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1208478_comment'></div>初，充之客寓宝应，茍营屋室，而勉竭其力，以择葬地于维扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1208478_comment'></div>躬诣内黄，启祖考之殡，迎护以来，将卜日历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1208478_comment'></div>盖奔走自效，服勤累岁，未克<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1208478", 1208478, "Clauses/94/Comments/0")'>迁奉</span>，而充之得疾卒矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1208478_comment'></div>今其子激等既葬充之，又能率先志，并襄大事，使三世窀穸之事讫无可憾，亦可以见充之身教之遗美矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1208478_comment'></div>激等遣人自宝应来南康，以吕本中所状充之之行求铭于瓘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1208478_comment'></div>书辞惨切，且曰：「先人疾亟时，尝问曰：『居仁约访我，尚未到』？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1208478_comment'></div>又叹曰：『我欲一游庐山，今不能矣』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1208478_comment'></div>诸孤不肖，摧割待尽，念欲毕闻馀训，永不可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1208478_comment'></div>维行状既获所属，而砻石穴土，以需于掩圹之后者，将孰请而可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1208478_comment'></div>居仁，本中字也，正献公之曾孙，言行有家法，其所叙次皆可考證。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1208478_comment'></div>其载充之教子之言曰：「涑水文正公尝谓平生无以过人，但事无大小皆可使人知尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1208478_comment'></div>汝曹不可一日忘此语也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1208478_comment'></div>濉阳刘公尝谓充之材用有馀，遽闻其死，嗟惜不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1208478_comment'></div>呜呼，可达可寿，而废斥夭短，岂非命欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1208478_comment'></div>其所厚善，率皆迟钝迂阔之士，于其殁也，能相与戚嗟而已，悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1208478_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_1208478'>木摇难栖，波涌莫济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1208478_comment'></div>穮蓘积劳，未穰而逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1208478_comment'></div>饥穰天也，人岂能违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1208478_comment'></div>奄忽不俟，岂唯我悲。</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1208478_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

淮安（山阳）
